Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
True Victory
Humanity is understood to have woven the history of the Fall. We also know that the living environment we are in today is a realm of the Fall, and thus we must go through the life course of the Fall.
Humanity surrounded by the realm of the Fall
Considering your current situation, if you are in your thirties or forties, you have gone through the process of life in the realm of the Fall to reach that age. And you are currently in such a position. Furthermore, there is a future that you must fight for as you look ahead to your life course. The past was like that, the present you are in is the same, and the future will also end up in a similar fate. Therefore, the question of how we will resolve the realm of the Fall cannot be overlooked.
In the past, there were attempts to escape from this realm of the Fall, and we are still trying to do so in the present, yet we are still surrounded by the realm of the Fall. Therefore, the question is how we will break through this encirclement in the future, how we will resolve this siege in the future. If we do not solve this problem ourselves, it is a matter that must be resolved through our descendants.
Victory within the realm of the Fall cannot be called true victory
We know better than anyone that human history began within the realm of the Fall and has been a history that has gone through the process of the Fall, solidifying the world of the consequences of the Fall.
When we think of an individual in such a world, even if that individual defeats numerous competitors and achieves some goal, they must transcend that environment to be victorious. Otherwise, even if they are guaranteed by that environment, the authority of that victory is merely a temporary authority. No matter how much they claim victory, that victory may remain limited to the individual or be a temporary victory, but it cannot be universalized. In other words, an individual victory cannot be matched to a family victory, nor can a family victory be expanded to represent a victory for a nation or state. Moreover, even if a state fights and wins against other states, that victory will remain as the victory of that one nation, but it cannot stand as a global or universal standard of victory.
When viewed in this light, today, in this era, the world is positioned beyond nations, centered around ideologies such as communism and democracy, and when they fight and one side claims victory as they wished, can that victory truly remain a global victory, or can it stand as a standard for all humanity to praise the glory of victory?
As you well know, even if communism were to dominate the world, there will always be areas within that victory that must be overthrown. Similarly, even if the democratic world claims the authority of victory, as long as remnants of the opposing world remain, there will need to be efforts to eliminate and overthrow that world centered around the democratic world.
When we look at the standard of victory in this way, regardless of whether the results of that victory are achieved through a direct confrontation process, there must be a struggle to digest that victory. Furthermore, regardless of the standard from which it was digested, the question remains whether what has been digested can become an eternal authority of victory, and in pursuing new theories and new practical lives, it will inevitably encounter limits that do not align with the entirety of humanity.
When we consider that even if all humanity has mobilized to bring about the results of victory they have pursued, can we definitively say that it can be praised forever and remain as a victorious value in front of the human world? The conclusion that it cannot exist within the realm of the Fall automatically arises.
Today, humans are engaged in a struggle from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world, all in the process of fighting to survive. They go through a competitive process without knowing what it is. However, even if they achieve the standard they desire through that competitive process, the joy they feel in celebrating that achievement is only joy at a certain limit. The value of that victory cannot be guaranteed for eternity, nor can it become a content of victory that the whole can affirm. That standard may serve as a temporary glory limited to the individual, but it cannot become a standard of glory for the whole that transcends history. This is a fact that you have seen and felt many times in your lives.
When someone studies and claims to have achieved their standard, can they adapt the value of that achievement to the entire field and utilize it as a factor? This is seen as an inevitable fact that it belongs within a very limited realm. Yet we know that human desires do not pursue only the value of victory within a limited realm.
The issue of individual victory becoming universal
When we think from a single point, if it serves as a motivation and is connected to the whole, we hope that that motivation or relationship with the whole does not remain limited to a restricted realm. Furthermore, if a certain victory has been determined, we desire that it acts as a foundation that can be utilized for the whole, resulting in the value of victory for the entire entity. From this perspective, we see that even if our individual entity achieves some success or fulfills some purpose, it is merely a result within a limited environment. With that alone, we cannot achieve completeness as humans.
Therefore, even if we claim victory, we must strive for a greater victory on that foundation of victory. It is the desire of humanity to strive for a greater victory that connects to the global stage. Because humanity has pursued and worked towards such desires, it is an inevitable conclusion that there must be a global end time.
Thus, when we have some standard of achievement that we desire in the global end time, and if there is something of greater value than that standard, we do not wish for our standard of victory to deviate from that. Centered on the foundation of ultimate victory, centered on eternity, and based on greater internal connections, we desire that the standard we have established for victory, which is not temporary but eternal, remains forever. The question arises whether there is indeed a standard that can allow for that.
When we consider philosophy today, we know it is a discipline that requires practical application centered around a theory. Therefore, we must practice, but what is the limit of that practice? It is the world. However, if we have practiced everything in the world, will that be the end? It will not be the end. Here, a new search and pursuit of new theoretical systems begins. In doing so, we reach the conclusion that the foundation of victory that has been cultivated until now cannot be guaranteed forever. When we consider this, the question arises whether the ideal world that humanity pursues, the eternal world that humanity seeks, and the world of happiness that humanity desires truly exists or not.
From this perspective, when we acknowledge that today’s world is within the realm of the Fall, the more we acknowledge it, the more we conclude that there is no way to absorb the content of a long-standing tradition as a foundation of victory within this realm of the Fall. I cannot universalize my victory. Without a specific content, universalization is impossible. Therefore, the ideal world that we humans seek cannot be found in a fallen world.
In this way, individual victories tend to end as partial victories. Thus, when it becomes impossible to universalize this, that is, when there is no content that can guarantee the victory of the whole, it will eventually pass away. Furthermore, it will disappear because it encounters results that people do not need.
Therefore, if that victory, whether individual, family, tribe, nation, or state, lacks the content to become a factor of the victory of the whole, a foundation, or a necessary condition, that victory will eventually vanish as a separate result.
Without true victory through true love, the ideal world cannot be manifested
If there is a God who says that this fallen world should not be fallen, what will that God bring to this world? What will be the factor that can leave a long-standing foundation of victory? From a human perspective, when we look at all beings in the world, there is matter, then there are people, and then there are hearts. So, what can people like? There will be matter. Then there are men and women. And among those people, there are hearts and bodies. However, when we look at the heart and body, we find that the heart and body are always in conflict.
When we consider our individual selves within the realm of the Fall, what is the most problematic? We need a field of life. To live, we need material conditions. Also, while things like food, clothing, and shelter are issues, emotional life is essential for humans. Hence, there is a counterpart. If there is a man, there is a woman. However, these men and women are fallen men and women. And the realm in which these men and women live is also a realm of the Fall. So, what would be an unfallen man and woman, or matter that is not within the realm of the Fall? We cannot help but think about these things.
If we say that we are unfallen humans and possess matter that is not within the realm of the Fall, then the matter related to our field of life will not be used and consumed from the standpoint of lamentation and sorrow. It may be used and consumed in the pursuit of more valuable content, but it will not be a consumption that sacrifices itself.
When we think about this, what would be the position of matter in an unfallen world and people in an unfallen world? If a person from an unfallen world has determined some victory, that victory must not be a temporary victory. That victory must be absorbed as a factor that can inherit a higher level of connection with the material world, and there must not be any conflict. Shouldn’t it be such matter or such people? If that is not possible, then the ideal world that humans pursue may exist as an individual ideal world, but the realized ideal world will not manifest.
Factors of victory and defeat
Then, what are the factors of defeat? The content within the realm of the Fall, its inner nature, will be the factor of defeat. Conversely, what will be the factor of victory? It will be something that is not related to the realm of the Fall.
From this perspective, where can we find the factors that can guarantee true victory? Will it be found within the realm of the Fall or in the realm that is not fallen? Today, since this world is already a fallen realm, no matter how much victory is claimed, it cannot be guaranteed as a complete authority of victory. Falling off a cliff and enjoying each other’s company, or falling off a cliff and exchanging with each other may indeed be a story of sympathy. However, no matter how good it is in such a situation, it cannot relate to or connect with the good position of not having fallen off the cliff.
So, where will we find the factors of defeat? The factors of defeat are fully present in the fallen world. Therefore, can we find the true factors of victory in the fallen world? That is impossible. They must be sought in a place that is not fallen.
When we look at the principles of the Unification Church, we can see that God created humans and all things. There can be no normal victory without following a normal trajectory. In this light, if God created humans and all things are connected through that person, then God is the core center, the person is the intermediary, and all things are at the outermost. Thus, the factors of victory cannot be solely based on humans. Where must this begin? It must inevitably start from God.
Then why is that? When we consider the direction humans should take, the content they should establish, and the foundation they should go through to pave the way for victory, if God exists, we must find the way that is closest, most reliable, and strongest connection to God. That must be the only way. Therefore, that path must first be determined.
Is that God’s work? Is it connected to our living realm centered on God’s work? It may be an external connection, but it will not be an internal connection. Then what is the standard of that internal connection?
in the relationship between God and true people. 

The essence of true victory lies in the connection between God and humanity. This connection is not merely a theoretical concept but a practical reality that manifests in our lives. 

When we seek happiness, we must recognize that it is not found in material wealth or external circumstances but in the emotional and spiritual connection we have with God and each other. This emotional bond is the foundation of our existence and the key to understanding our purpose.

In our pursuit of happiness, we must also acknowledge the importance of relationships. The dynamics of these relationships, whether hierarchical or horizontal, shape our experiences and guide our interactions. God, as our Father, desires a relationship with us that transcends mere obedience; He seeks a mutual connection that fosters growth and understanding.

As we navigate our lives, we must strive to align our hearts and minds with God's will. This alignment is essential for achieving true unity and harmony within ourselves and with others. When our hearts resonate with God's love, we can experience profound joy and fulfillment.

In a world often marked by division and conflict, it is crucial to recognize the importance of emotional integrity and the need for genuine relationships. Our happiness and success depend on our ability to connect with others and to cultivate a spirit of love and understanding.

Ultimately, true victory is found in our relationship with God and in our ability to embody His love in our interactions with others. By embracing this truth, we can overcome the challenges of our fallen world and achieve a lasting sense of fulfillment and purpose.
Where is the standard, the boundary, the limit? It is the male god. God is the Father, and we are called His sons. However, while this serves as a vertical standard, it does not serve as a horizontal standard. 

Therefore, you must stand in a position equal to God, and from an internal perspective, we must stand in a relative position to God's heart. When you hold this as a hope... the starting point for the vertical heart of God's creation to be represented horizontally is to seek a counterpart. This is speaking from the center of the heart. Adolescence is about speaking from the center of the heart. 

We must establish the standard of victory in glory, where no one can invade that family centered on such couples and such sons and daughters. If there is no such standard, ideals cease to exist. There cannot be an ideal centered on the individual. There must be an ideal centered on the family. Since we live as human beings belonging to a family, individual ideals are unnecessary. Even without individual ideals, if the ideal realm of the family is established, the world will begin to take shape from there. Finding that starting point from this perspective is the foundation of the heart issue in Unification Thought and the theory of the ideal family. With this alone, God...

The place where this is determined must not be separated from God. God must always be present. Because God is present, the joy He felt regarding Adam, the joy He felt regarding Eve, and the joy He felt regarding sons and daughters always exists. Isn’t that so? Therefore, one cannot have a negative view of the father, nor of the wife, nor of the children. Similarly, can a child have a negative view of God?

Our Unification Church thought is centered on the ideal family, and what can be the foundation of that thought? It is God's heart. It is both the beginning and the process, and it is both the process and the result. That result is not a negative one but a joyful one.

To achieve victory, one must be willing to give up everything and die. 

So where does the ideal world begin? It does not start from any nation. It starts from the family. Then what will happen to the fallen world? It cannot be based on the fallen world. However, the issue here is why God has led humanity to abandon the world, the nation, the family, parents, siblings, and even themselves up to this end time. It is not to lead us to ruin. It is to find us. It is to return and seek. It is to find the external.

Then who must be found first? Should the external world be found first, or should religious people be found first? Religious people must be found first. 

Recently, the Jesus Revolution movement emerged, right? The religious hippies. It is an interesting phenomenon. Currently, as the external hippies are coming to an end, the internal hippies have emerged. The Jesus Revolution... Yesterday, the teacher asked the members who came from America about it. They said that those groups called the Jesus Revolution are like Jesus's hippies? The world is really interesting. Seeing this, I believe our intention will spread more and more. (Laughter)

So what will come at the end? A revolutionary will come, right? A revolutionary has no place. Is there a place for revolution? Do they establish a position to revolutionize? There is no place. They wander around. From this perspective, when comparing non-religious people and religious people, in this situation where everyone is abandoning everything, religious people must not just criticize and judge those hippies. They must go beyond that. They must abandon the world, the nation, parents, children, and then themselves...

While the world of Satan is opening its mouth in despair, the side of heaven must endure. One side may fall, but the other side is determined to win. The world is now in despair, having lost everything. Who made this situation? God made it this way, and even if we lose everything in that situation, we must go out and say, "God, thank you. I lost the world, but I found myself." 

Isn’t that ultimately about finding Adam? Isn’t it about finding Eve? In the end, we must say, "God, I lost only myself, but I found everything else." And when we can claim that we found everything and lost ourselves, isn’t that when we can qualify to inherit the world from here? Do you understand? 

Thus, we must have the heart that says, "Even if the world is given to me, I cannot exchange it; even if a nation is given to me, I cannot exchange it; even if a family is given to me, I cannot exchange it; I cannot exchange myself for anything." We must have that heart. We must have a day where we can stand at the forefront that can urge my self-awareness and affirm my whole being with God's joy. Without such a day for humans living under the fallen realm, there can be no hope. Have you experienced that? Look. The hippies of the world are playing games where they abandon their dignity and status, but today, Christianity is using dignity and status... for other purposes. Such dignity and status tainted by Satan... While people within the religious authority of the world do such things, Unification Church members cannot engage in such games. Do you understand?

The world is at that point, yet those who should embrace and lead it must be the religious people. However, they must not follow what the world has done and say they cannot do it. Can you stand in the midst of the factors of victory while holding onto that?

From this perspective, the words of Jesus are correct. "Those who seek to save their lives will lose them, and those who lose their lives will save them," "I did not come to bring peace to the earth, but a sword," "Your household members are your enemies" — these words fit perfectly.

While the world speaks of hippies, we must become the hippies of the heart. We must become the hippies of the heart. Do you understand what I mean? Where has the loyalty of those who love their nation gone in this earthly realm? Where has the loyalty of those who love their parents gone? Where has the loyalty of those who advocated for love gone? Where has it gone? The center of the nation is God, the center of the world is God, the center of morality is God, and the center of my life must also be God. Before such God, we must... Discovering oneself in that way will develop a new worldview. In that development, as we connect with God, the unfallen emotional and principled relationships will be established with men and women, and from there, a new world of victory will begin.

When my individual heart and body unite and I go through the adolescent stage to take a counterpart, that cannot be a factor of defeat. It can be said to be mine forever and ever. The sons and daughters found there will not become factors of fall and despair but will become factors of pride. My sons and daughters must become factors of pride forever, but they have not. Thus, the established lineage will not remain as factors of despair, lamentation, and division but will remain as factors of pride, unity, and oneness. It will be as one heart.

Therefore, in the future, Unification Church members must ultimately go through God. That is the conclusion. In the end, we must go through God. In the realm of the super-sensory, while there may not be a super-sensory heart, when we transcend the fallen sensory world and acquire the origin of our inherent senses, and when we praise that happiness, the world can be rendered insignificant. We are willing to sacrifice our nation and the world for this... Because the nation and the world do not exist before this is achieved.

Therefore, we must seek this even if it means abandoning the world. The nation and the world manifest on the foundation of love. However, the existence of a nation or world is non-principled. Thus, it is only natural to reach the result of negation. Therefore, to seek true love, we must abandon the world. That love speaks of true love. It is not speaking of worldly love. While love may seem good, until now, it has been a love that breaks apart. Here, we are not speaking of such love.

From this perspective, before humans possess true love, there are no families or sons and daughters. Before having a family of true love, there are no tribes, no nations, and no world. Isn’t that so? The nation and the world begin from the center of true love. Therefore, the sons and daughters born there are those who can dominate the world, and those tribes are those who can manage the world.

Centered on this foundation, the realm of the ideal family is established (as he writes while speaking) God, Adam, Eve... When the center is firmly established and love is exchanged, it turns. Isn’t that so? When the center is established and love is exchanged, it turns.

Look at a top. When you spin a top, if the center is firmly held, it spins alive. If the center is not held, it spins for a while and then quickly falls over. It is the same. The position of a perfect center lasts longer. (Due to poor recording conditions, some parts could not be organized.)

The core of Unification Church's restoration thought is why God created Adam. It was to feel the stimulating relative love of both vertical and horizontal dimensions. Unilateral love is not ideal love. It is not interesting. Only when it connects and turns in all directions can the thrill and sweetness according to the 360-degree direction change. This is ideal love. Isn’t that so? This is not a plane but a sphere. When it becomes a sphere and moves, there is no separate God, and there is no separate spirit world. It becomes one. It becomes a world of oneness.

The high becomes me, not someone else. The subject and object must become one for that world to become the ideal world. The high is always high, and the low is always low.

God is an incorporeal being. He became corporeal through Adam because He cannot remain incorporeal. Form is something that must be felt through the relationship between subject and object.

Therefore, a person must unite as man and woman, that is, subject and object, for completion to occur. God's completion also happens when the invisible inner God and the external Adam and Eve unite, becoming one both internally and externally, allowing the inner form to replace the outer form and vice versa, so God can take on a form and stand as the center of humanity.

So what will happen? To feel the sweetness of love in a three-dimensional world is God's ideal of creation, and the heavenly kingdom is a world built on love. Therefore, the distance of proximity and distance is determined according to the standard that can adapt to the sensitivity of love.

When you look at a tree, a tree that receives a lot of sunlight grows quickly. Isn’t that so? It becomes lush quickly. Such a tree will bloom many flowers and bear many fruits. It is the same. Therefore, from the perspective of absorbing the sensitivity of love, it is like that trunk. The love factors that the whole can feel pass through it, allowing it to feel the joy of love corresponding to that field and environment. The result of that joy becomes the standard of joy that corresponds to God's overall joy and determines the relationship between God and me.

In light of these issues, we want to leave such victories for tomorrow. So where is the standard of that victory? It is with women. This is why religion has not allowed the relative world until now. We must seek again. Because we have returned to the position of finding such a God, we will acknowledge the relative world. For those in that position, the relative ideal world will be permitted...

Because the Unification Church is in the position to inherit that, you have been blessed. So, have you, who are blessed, truly stood in the position of the perfected Adam and Eve? No, you have not. Therefore, it must be indemnified. There must be a process of indemnifying by binding together the nations of the world. This is the process of indemnification that must be pursued after the seven-year period.

What is the purpose of you going through that process of indemnification? You must stand on a family foundation that can be better than the original parents. This is the standard that Unification families look toward. From that perspective, you cannot remain in your current state as it is. There needs to be a new negation and reform.

The reason I have fought and won in leading the Unification Church until now is not to leave behind a temporary, passing standard of victory. It is to leave behind an eternal victory. It is to stand in that place that remains forever. With whom? With God. Therefore, although I fought as an individual, the standard of that victory remains forever.

In the historical process, establishing such a standard of victory is the restoration thought of our Unification Church. Therefore, you must be better than the fallen Adam and Eve. You must be better than Abel. Or if it is Noah, you must be better than Noah, and you must be better than Abraham. You must be better than them. Isn’t that so? You must be better than Moses. You must be better than John the Baptist. You must be better than Jesus. (The remainder could not be organized due to poor recording conditions.) 

The path of Jesus to take
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is the last day of October and also the Sabbath. As we think about this day, which marks the end of one month and the beginning of a new one, I earnestly hope that the passing days will provide important opportunities for our lives and paths. 

As I think about how much we long to become trustworthy leaders before the nation You desire, and how the bond of life between You and us can be reestablished, we feel that we are always indebted to You while living on this earth. 

Please look down upon Your children gathered here this morning. As we reflect on the fact that we were originally meant to be Your sons and daughters who revere You, we cannot help but lament our lowly, base, and wicked descendants when we yearn for that holy position of being Your sons and daughters, which cannot be exchanged for anything in the universe. 

Even though we were meant to start from goodness, we were born rooted in an unwanted foundation of evil. We realize that without Your infinite compassion being with us, we cannot even have hope. 

This morning, please come and be with us. The individual circumstances...
Even if we are different, the heart that misses you must be the same. Your son,  
I cannot deny the fact that I want to be your son and daughter.  
When I think that this is the wish you desire and should be a standard of our wishes,  
our birth is for this purpose, living is for this purpose, and even the way we live our lives is for this purpose. Please allow us to dedicate our entire lives to this purpose.  
Now, please look after the young children gathered in your presence. The owner of this place is only you. I know that the one who will bind our life’s connection here is only you.  
Let us return to the heart of a child, and like a child longing for their mother’s milk, may our hearts rise up to yearn before heaven. We must become those who can feel and seek to align with the feelings you cherish, which we miss and long for.  
When I think of the past, I feel that I cannot hide my shame before you, and I cannot help but feel how inadequate my current self is to present before you. Please take all of this upon yourself. Hold us with something that is worthy in your sight and can align with the wishes you desire, and lead us to that place.  
May the heart that wishes to dedicate everything capture all of our hearts, and may our desire to be remembered before you become earnest.  
In our life’s journey, we should rely solely on you, our Father, yet we are aware that living on this wicked earth often leads us to live in ways you do not desire. Therefore, Father, please extend your hand of mercy and compassion, allowing us to live a life that can achieve the final victory and be a life of true living.  
On this day, Father, as we enter the last day of October, please be with us. Tomorrow we will face a new month and a new day. We must not let the passing time be in vain. Whether we face tribulations or stand at the forefront to fight, we must feel that we cannot leave behind anything without establishing a connection with you and receiving your compassion. If there has been a life lived with you until now, Father, I earnestly hope you will come once more to encourage us, allow us to stand as the sons you need before the wishes you desire, and let us remain as your daughters.  
Father, the year 1971 was the year we swore before you. We vowed to make this year an important one in history. Now, we have passed this October. What will you present to us in the remaining two months?  
Father, you must protect your children scattered across the nation, including the Seoul Church. Please allow us to be the sons and daughters needed before all providential paths, and let us become heavenly warriors who can protect your battlefield. I earnestly wish for us to be children who can gather your heart in your family and symbolize your joy.  
Father, until now, you have protected us. Please extend your gracious hand so that we may remain unscathed until the end, fulfilling our responsibilities as your sons and daughters.  
We, gathered here, have not prepared anything. With our shortcomings, we come before you, extending our weak hands towards you. Father, please hold us. Feeling guilt over our inadequacies, we seek your compassion. Father, please come to us personally and reign over our hearts and bodies, extending your hand of new creation to remove everything that is not in accordance with your will, allowing us to harmonize with you and remain with you.  
At this time, please hold all your children gathered here in your palm, allowing us to take on the mission you wish to entrust to us before your desired will, and let us become heavenly soldiers who can guard the final front line and praise the glory of victory without lacking anything.  
I earnestly wish for this.  
At this time, may your children scattered across the nation look up to this place, and may you personally join them in their sincere efforts. Moreover, please remember the young daughters who are on the front lines. I earnestly hope that you will see all they desire and all they sincerely strive for with compassion.  
They know well for whom they stand in such a place. They are stepping forward not only for this nation and this people but also for the suffering humanity of this era. Please allow them to have strong and valuable steps.  
Even though they bear the responsibilities of the historical age, if they fail to fulfill that responsibility, they will inevitably become miserable and pitiful beings who are accused by their ancestors, humanity, and descendants. Knowing this, Father, please help them to maintain their current position, affirm their current victory, and become daughters who are fully devoted to manifesting your glory in every moment.  
Through them, please look upon the established churches that must be set before this people with compassion. It is the principle that without the unity of Cain and Abel, there is no way to proceed. Therefore, the Unification Church must inevitably unite with the established churches. Without this unity, there is no way to save this nation. When we think that the path to unity is the path of principle and that your providence is proceeding according to this principle, please help each of us to fulfill the grave mission entrusted to us.  
Please allow this church to fulfill its responsibilities, and I earnestly hope that you will protect and nurture this church so that it can carry this pitiful nation within your will.  
When we think about how much you long for the country of wishes that all beings desire to be realized, we must have a unified Korea, both North and South. When we think of this, Father, we must not let our days pass in vain. We must live in a way that can fully devote ourselves to fulfilling the mission you have entrusted to us, with all our loyalty. We must understand that this life cannot be achieved without going through the repeated struggles. I earnestly hope that you will allow your children to deeply and greatly feel this in their hearts.  
Looking at the future world situation, I earnestly hope that you will discuss with humanity the path that Korea can take, the path that Asia can take, and the path that the world can take, and pave the way forward.  
In this journey, the ones who must become the heavenly vanguard are not those who are elsewhere. When we think that there is your will to hide this significant mission through your children gathered here, who may seem insignificant, and through the Unification Church scattered alone, Father, please do not forsake us. I earnestly hope that you will lead us by standing at the forefront.  
Thus, may this denomination, which bears responsibility before this people, fulfill its duties and be allowed to escape shame before you. We must not become those who are accused by future generations for failing to fulfill the remaining national mission. Therefore, Father, please allow us to whip our bodies and minds to fulfill our responsibilities with all our sincerity and heart.  
On this morning, may you bless every place where your children are gathered, and please watch over the many families that belong to you, calling you Father. In this final age, as we become the people of one nation and citizens, may your guidance ensure that not a single person is left behind, allowing them to become heavenly families.  
Please look upon this gathering of inadequate beings. This is not a place where we have come looking at anyone else. We have come here longing for you and earnestly seeking your heart. Now, please allow this time to be one where we can convey your deep heart to us and communicate our heartfelt wishes to you, allowing us to harmonize with you.  
I earnestly wish for this.  
Please be with us in the remaining time, and remember your children scattered across the world who gather in your name.  
I earnestly hope and wish that your glory, victory, and authority may be manifested upon this earth.  
I earnestly request that you preside over this time, and I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> We know that all humans living on this earth have set their own standards to live by. We understand that both the talented and the less fortunate, in their own way, seek their own purposes in today’s human affairs. This is true for individuals, organizations, and nations alike. Furthermore, it must also be true for the world as a whole.  
When we look at the place we desire, centered on our current situation, we recognize that there are people like A and people like B, and since each person's circumstances differ, they each seek their own purposes from their own situations.  
Looking at the historical process, we know that through specific individuals, the hopes and purposes that everyone can aspire to are manifested in the lives of those who live according to them, and history is directed toward one place through this. Thus, whether it is a talented person, someone with great thoughts, or someone who follows the heavenly fortune, or someone who possesses a higher ideal, we understand that the paths they walk are implicitly viewed as standards in the course of history.  
If there is a historical purpose that can remain eternally in the course of history, when the internal connections or external circumstances align with that purpose, the wishes of the figures established in that historical course can remain as a standard for humanity over centuries or thousands of years. Among them, the specific individuals we admire are the saints.  
When we look at these saints, we know that those who do not introduce heaven or think of the world centered on heaven cannot become saints. We understand that all saints are representatives of the religions they lead.  
In other words, they are not in a position to represent only humanity; they have a connection with heaven and seek a purpose that is not limited to their immediate surroundings but aims to achieve the true overall purpose as the last humans until the end of humanity. All saints have invested their lives to align with that purpose, and we know through history that they have been leading humanity along that path through the religions they have established.  
In other words, no matter how great an individual's wish may be, if they do not seek a path that can align with heaven, that individual will come to a halt. No matter how strong a nation may be, when it reaches a limit where it cannot inherit a global nation or a global ideological system, that nation will inevitably perish.  
From this perspective, when we consider what the highest purpose that a saint can aspire to is, that saint must be someone who cannot help but represent humanity.  
What drives humanity centered on human ethics? It is human affection. One must be able to stand in a position that can represent humanity, equipped with both human ethics and affection, and be able to replace the world's purpose as a representative of humanity. Not only that, but if there is a heavenly principle, if there is a path that heaven seeks, one must be able to stand in a position that represents the heavenly principle and, in the providential course that replaces heaven, maintain the position of the heavenly principle that represents the individual and stand in the position that represents the heavenly principle of a nation and the world, while also being able to represent heaven.  
In other words, one must be someone who can represent both human ethics and affection, as well as heavenly principles and the heavenly realm, while simultaneously representing both heaven and humanity.  
Who is such a person? When we look at it centered on God’s love, that person must be the one closest to God. When viewed from the perspective of heaven, if there is a family in the heavenly nation, that person must be the central being of that family.  
If there is a nation in the heavenly kingdom, that person must be the central being of that nation, and if there is a world in the heavenly kingdom, that person must be the central being of that world. Furthermore, they must stand in the position of a global representative in the family and be the center that can represent the world among nations.  
They must also be the center that represents the entire world.  
It is not about being a center that is separated from the human world and the heavenly world; rather, it is about being a center that can represent the whole from a position where human ethics and heavenly principles are united, where human affection and the heavenly realm intersect. Without such a person, an individual cannot establish a global standard that represents the world. Nor can they establish a global central being that can represent a nation. Nor can they appear as a central being that can represent the world. That individual center must represent the entire heavenly kingdom, and the center of the nation must represent the center of the heavenly kingdom, and the center of the world must manifest as a center that represents the entire heavenly kingdom.  
That person is the center of the world, the center of the nation, and the center of the individual. They are the one who has united the heavenly principles and the heavenly realm, or human ethics and human affection, as an individual, or who can unite them on behalf of a nation.
is the person who can unite on behalf of the world. In this way, from one to the whole, without separating human morality and heavenly morality, or human affection and heavenly sentiment, one must be able to follow a single trajectory, leaving a mark on their life course, and manifesting it in their living environment. We cannot help but think that such a person must emerge. By meeting that person, humanity can look forward to the completion of its history. When viewed in terms of human affection and love, that person can occupy a central position in this world more than anyone else, and not only end at the central position but also stand in a place that can evoke heavenly sentiment.

The Wish of Jesus
When we look at it this way, who has borne such responsibility in history? We can say it is Jesus Christ. When he spoke on behalf of God and humanity, he said, "I am the only begotten Son of God." He said, "I am the only Son of God." The term "only begotten" means the first person who can receive love before God. The only begotten is the representative who can receive all of God's love. From the perspective of the individual, he emphasized his position as one who stood in a representative position to receive love before God more than anyone else.

This was something that no one in the historical era could declare, but we know that Jesus was the foremost person in representing heavenly sentiment and human affection. 

The Path Jesus Must Take
He does not end at the position of receiving God's love but must stand in the position of the bridegroom concerning humanity. All believers who followed and revered Jesus went through a public life similar to that of Jesus to establish a relationship as the bride. The bride and bridegroom referred to here are not centered on human affection and morality but rather on heavenly sentiment and heavenly morality.

Then Jesus said, "Those who believe in me will not be servants but friends," and furthermore, "They will be brothers." 

When we see this, what is the core of the doctrine that Jesus advocated? It is to stand in the position of a son who can receive God's love, and as such a son, to establish a family that God desires, which is undoubtedly a fact. 

It is not centered on human morality and affection but rather adds heavenly morality and sentiment, centering on a worldview that can be recognized by God, and based on a providential view, personally being a son of God, being the head of a family, and in terms of living, establishing brotherly connections, which is also God's wish for Jesus and the mission that Jesus had to fulfill on this earth.

The Path Jesus Must Walk
So, when we consider the issue of the path Jesus must take, what kind of path is it? It is the path of the only begotten who must uphold the way to receive God's love. Receiving God's love is not limited to the youth and young adulthood but must continue through middle age and old age, and of course, while on this earth, but also standing in the position to receive God's love eternally in the afterlife, completing that path is the path Jesus must take.

From the moment of his birth, Jesus stood in the position to receive God's love, and he had to be born in a place where God could rejoice, and he had to grow up in an environment where he could receive God's love. He must live in an environment where he receives God's love throughout his youth, middle age, and old age. Even after completing his life course as a human, it must still be so.

When we think about this, we realize that while God loved Jesus from the time he was born through his life course, there was no individual who represented the humans who loved Jesus. Today, we members of the Unification Church know that such a person did not exist. Who was the individual who truly loved Jesus? It was not Joseph. Of course, Mary loved him from the standpoint of a mother, but in terms of love, it was easy to love from a human-centered perspective; did she stand in the position to love from the standpoint of representing heavenly sentiment from the moment of his birth throughout his life course? We know that she did not.

We know what Jesus said to his mother at the wedding feast in Cana of Galilee: "Woman, what do I have to do with you?" The fact that he said something that a human could not say indicates that he bore a sorrow that could not be expressed to anyone.

Considering the family background, Jesus was born at the stage where Joseph and Mary were engaged, so his father, from a worldly perspective today, is seen as a stepfather. Jesus grew up in the care of a stepfather. Between Joseph and Mary, Jesus was always more of a subject of doubt than a source of joy; he was undoubtedly a being who caused emotional conflicts.

Was there a father who could rejoice in Jesus? We know that there was not. Did he have a mother who could rejoice in him? We know that there was not.

We can see through the Bible that there were always troubles and issues arising between Joseph and Mary because of Jesus.

When we consider Jesus' heart, if he was born as a son who could represent heavenly sentiment, then that heavenly sentiment should not have been confined to Jesus himself. The love of God that he received as the only begotten should not have been limited to himself. That love should have been horizontally connected to his father, and if it was his mother, it should have been completely connected to her. In connecting love centered on parents, he should have also connected it to siblings, relatives, the church, and even the nation of Israel. If Jesus had connected that love horizontally, he would not have died.

Then, as the Son of God, as the only begotten of God, was there anyone who directly poured out all of his love saying, "This is my love" to humanity? When we look at the Bible, we can find sorrowful accounts.

When Jesus began his public ministry at the age of 30 and sought out his disciples, when we look at Peter, James, John, or the twelve disciples, were they indeed the objects of longing that Jesus wanted to love in the human world? We know that they were not. Those disciples were not people of authority in the upper class of that time, nor were they a group that could be respected in the external environment.

When Jesus came to this earth and went through his public ministry, he was labeled a friend of tax collectors and a person who enjoyed eating and drinking. He preferred to dwell with sinners and enjoyed being with them, as we know from the biblical records. In this regard, the people Jesus interacted with were not representatives that everyone in that era could respect. The tax collectors who were despised in that era and Jesus' fishermen friends stood in the position of friends. Were they not all uneducated people? You know this well from reading the Bible.

The twelve apostles today stand in a position we can respect, but this was established as a standard proportional to the development of Christianity and the Christian cultural sphere in the historical process; at the time of Jesus, they were nothing.

Having gone through three years of public ministry, when Jesus stood on the path to the cross, all the disciples whom he loved deeply abandoned him. Was there a true disciple who could swear to die with Jesus when he was walking the path to death? Even Peter, who swore steadfastly that he would not abandon the teacher even if all the others did, stood in the position of denying him three times. Knowing this, could Jesus truly stand in a position to love the twelve disciples, including his chief disciple Peter, with the heart of heavenly sentiment? It is natural that Jesus could not stand in a position to genuinely love humanity as a true son connected to God's heart.

How lonely must Jesus have felt when he looked at the disciples who abandoned him before the cross? He came to this earth to receive love, but also to give love. Yet, when he tried to love, there was no one to love, and when he tried to receive love, there was no one to give love. In such a position, he had to walk the lonely path of the cross; who could have understood the lonely heart of Jesus? No one knew. No one could comprehend that.

Standing in such a position, carrying the cross and approaching the place of death, if there had been even one person on this earth who could have drawn a picture of that moment of overcoming hardship in his heart, if there had been one object of love who could have struggled and said, "I must also walk the path you are walking for Jesus," the path of the death of the cross would not have been such a lonely path.

In the extreme of loneliness, on the path of death alongside the criminals on either side, when the criminal on the right comforted him with a few words and said, "You will be with me in paradise today," it was not a joyful moment but rather a moment of extreme loneliness for Jesus, who had come to this earth to leave behind a part of human affection. He had to leave behind some emotional connection with the criminal on the right, and if he had not done so, he would have felt there was no way to return to the human world to find love. When we think about the fact that he stood in a position to sympathize with the criminal on the right, how miserable was that? 

Jesus did not come to this earth to meet just one criminal on the right; that is an absurd statement. After 4,000 years of sending many prophets and saints to nurture and raise the nation of Israel, it was not to leave behind Judaism itself, nor was it to leave behind the nation of Israel itself. It was solely for Jesus. The nation remained because Jesus remained, and the denomination remained because Jesus remained; the nation of Israel and Judaism were established by God for the sake of Jesus, not for any denomination or nation that could remain apart from Jesus.

That nation rebelled, and that denomination pushed him toward death, and in a lonely position where even his parents did not truly love him, in a serious path of death where even his disciples rejected him, who was the one who could leave behind a word of sympathy? It was the criminal on the right.

Did God send Jesus to meet that criminal on the right? No, that is not the case. Jesus, who was receiving God's love on behalf of the entire nation and representing God's heartfelt love, wanted to love from the position where God wanted to love the entire nation.

Was it not Jesus' wish to love those who remained after enduring the path of suffering with the connection of God's love he received? Did he not want to love the entire lineage of Joseph and the lineage of Zechariah, and all his relatives, standing in the position of a son receiving God's love, wanting to love that lineage? Furthermore, did he not want to love his parents and beloved siblings with the heart of love that received God's love, embracing them as his brothers and parents? When we look at it this way, when did Jesus ever have such love? He never experienced love. Jesus was one who could not love.

When we think about this, it is clear that God did not orchestrate this path of death for Jesus. That is without question. After dying on the cross and resurrecting three days later, when Jesus went to find the scattered disciples, that path was not a joyful one for him. Before his death, he had to establish emotional connections on this earth, but no one could establish those connections in the place God had prepared. After sweeping away this foundation, the connections were made only after his resurrection. Was there anyone who could love him right after he resurrected? There was no one who could love him.

When Mary Magdalene went to the tomb of Jesus, she met the resurrected Jesus. At first, she thought he was the gardener, but later realized he was the Lord and was delighted to hold onto him, but he refused her, saying not to do so. Why was that? There is an order to love. Jesus should have loved his mother and father, then loved his siblings, then loved his relatives, then loved the church, then loved the nation, and finally loved the world. There must be an order to love.

In the resurrection, the one who should have come with the most earnest heart should have been Jesus' mother, father, and siblings, and they should have been his disciples. Yet, when we see the appearance of a woman before Jesus, it must have been shocking.

After the resurrection, Jesus stood to gather the disciples who had betrayed him for 40 days. As the day of his departure drew near, Jesus asked Peter, "Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?" Peter replied, "Lord, you know that I love you." When Jesus asked again, "Simon, son of John, do you love me?" Peter answered vaguely, "Lord, you know that I love you." The first time he answered with his face raised, but when Jesus asked him seriously a second time, did Peter have confidence in his heart? That is the question.

Did Peter respond with a firm confidence, saying, "No matter what comes my way, I love you. Even if heaven and earth shake, my heart to love you cannot be broken"? Or was he standing in a conflicted position, feeling the weight of having denied Jesus three times just a few days earlier? When he answered the third time, "Lord, you know that I love you," he certainly did not answer with his face raised but rather with his head bowed. Don't you think so? The one who had denied him three times stood before the very person who asked him, "Do you love me?"
You do not know how much I love you. No matter what opposes it, I will break everything down and remove everything, and can you really ask the master, "Is this not so?" in such a confident position? When asked twice and three times, was it not Peter who could only lower his head more and more?

When we think like this, we must understand that in Jesus' question, "Do you love me more than these?" lies the ultimate intention to conclude the life of Jesus, who was extremely lonely. As the Son of God, who was to monopolize God's love and pour it all out for humanity, who did he love on this earth? The place where he claimed to have loved became instead a place where he asked if he was loved. How miserable is this position? Christianity, which cannot have an apostle who can praise him after the resurrection with the words, "Simon, son of John, I know that you love me more than these," is a miserable religion. It cannot be seen any other way. Jesus, who could not have such a disciple, was a Jesus who could not even love his disciples. So, who could he love?

Mary and Joseph's inability to take responsibility and Jesus leaving home
Mary knows well what she could not take responsibility for, and we know that Joseph, as a stepfather, made life difficult for Jesus. We also know that relatives pointed fingers and cursed him upon hearing rumors that Jesus was an illegitimate child.

When you look at the Bible, there is a record of Jesus, at the age of twelve, going up to the temple in Jerusalem and discussing with the priests and teachers of the law. The Bible records this as a good thing. Why was that? It is certain that when Joseph and Mary went to the temple in Jerusalem, they took Jesus with them. As parents, Joseph and Mary had to watch over the young Jesus and move with him. Yet, they went back to their hometown for three days and only then met Jesus. They left him in the temple for three days... The parents returned to their hometown, but why did they return? Do you think they returned happily? There was trouble because of Jesus.

When Joseph asked Mary who the father of Jesus was, that was when the problem arose. What man would not question the father of that child? Of course, Joseph brought Mary home through God's revelation, but what man would not ask who the father was when the woman gave birth to a child she did not know? The trouble continued.

In that gap, Jesus, knowing that he could not fulfill his purpose, left home. He abandoned his home. The three years of public ministry were not to be a loudmouth spreading rumors in the neighborhood, nor to be labeled as an instigator before the church and the nation. If Joseph and Mary had created an environment where the purpose could be fulfilled without anyone knowing, the purpose would have been achieved, but because Joseph and Mary could not take responsibility, Jesus ended up on the cross.

The path Jesus had to take
From the time Jesus was in the womb, there were rumors in the village about the discord between Joseph and Mary. Wouldn't that be the case? The news that the child in Mary's womb was not Joseph's spread throughout the village even before he was born. Therefore, even relatives treated Jesus as a stepson and did not regard him as a person.

Because Jesus could not be born in such a village, God had no choice but to have him born in a place like Bethlehem, where no one knew. Jesus was born in Bethlehem, but there were no grandparents present. The distance from Bethlehem to Jerusalem is only a short distance.

With such a sad background, who would know that the disciples wrote the Bible? Today, Christians do not know the facts buried in the twists and turns. Because the Unification Church has come out at this time to reveal such unknown facts, Christianity has been able to greet a bright new morning.

Look. The fact that Jesus asked his disciples, "Do you love me more than these?" is so miserable. God must have wished that you could say, "You loved me more than these." Jesus' desire was to meet someone who could say that, but where did he find such a person? Did he meet them through his family, through his mother and father? No, he did not. Did he meet them through his siblings? No, he did not. Did he meet them through his clan? No, he did not. Did he meet them through his church? No, he did not. Did he meet them through the nation of Israel? No, he did not. Did he meet them through the rulers and authorities of that nation, or through the teachers of the law in the church? No, he did not. 

He had no choice but to seek out the utterly lowly fishermen, not even the middle class. Even now, in South Korea, if you are a fisherman, you are not treated as a person; how much less so 2,000 years ago? When you go to the shores of Galilee, it is laughable. If you visit the house where Peter lived, it is a cave.

The situation was dire. In such a world, the very miserable crowd, unable to spread the bonds of love on earth with all their heart before dying, were pushed to the last wish of Jesus' three years of public ministry.

The miserable path of Jesus' public ministry
Today, Christians think of it as a holy path... and believe they will go to heaven? Jesus' public ministry was not a holy path but a miserable one. It was the moment when the 4,000-year history of Israel was turned upside down, the moment when the history of Judaism was shattered, and the moment when the foundation of blessings in Joseph's family was blown apart. The connections with the disciples were all torn apart, and it was a moment without hope.

However, because Jesus, as the Son of God, had to bind God's love with humanity, how to connect this remained as a foundation of resentment even after his death. Jesus, who had to go and express his situation to the disciples who betrayed him, who would have known that? It was a shocking scene. When we see this, we realize that Jesus could not love anyone during his time on earth. Thus, he managed things centered around the twelve disciples who betrayed him.

Because they drove Jesus, who came to find the bonds of love, to the path of death, such a crowd must be punished. In order to seek God's love, the path Jesus took to leave behind the bond of God's love was the path of the cross, so those who seek to inherit God's love must walk the path of the cross. The cross did not arise as a means of salvation; it is the way of suffering in Christianity. You must understand that.

What? You say you will be saved by the cross? Without going through the cross, without going through the way of suffering, you cannot be saved. Because he walked that path, you cannot find the place where you could have loved unless you follow that path. You cannot find the place of Peter before he said he loved. Peter's position is not before Jesus died but after he died, so the history of Christianity for the past 2,000 years has been about seeking a promise of love after his death.

Until now, Christians have believed that Jesus is the bridegroom and they are the brides. Many prophets and saints have gone through the trials of martyrdom, but they could not meet Jesus before they died and say, "My beloved bridegroom, pour out your love upon me." Can love that could not be expressed while alive be expressed after death? That is why those who believe in Christianity are miserable. To spiritually meet Jesus, one must walk the path of suffering for more than seven years. More than seven years; can someone who believes in Jesus spiritually meet him? Not a chance. After exhausting all their strength, they must find the authority of resurrection and become participants in it, and only by passing through the place where they could have established the bonds of love before Jesus was crucified can they elevate themselves to the position of the thief on the right side, or even higher. Therefore, it is said that those who seek to live will die, and those who seek to die will live. To believe in Jesus and be saved, one must be prepared to die. Only by standing in the position of Peter after overcoming the brink of death can one receive the promise of love and return; it cannot happen before that.

We must understand the astonishing circumstances of Jesus
So, what was Jesus' sorrow? Was he happy to meet Jesus after the resurrection? While there was joy, there was also sorrow behind it, and you must understand this. The purpose of God sending Jesus was not for him to die and then resurrect to ask the disciples, "Do you love me?" This was not God's wish.

To prevent this, how much effort did God put in to preserve Judaism and the nation of Israel? The foundation prepared for the son, fearing he might suffer, was shattered into pieces... Leading the most miserable of people, God intended to fulfill his wish again, but in the midst of that, Jesus was often rejected and died, and we must understand the astonishing circumstances under which he broke the tomb and returned to fulfill his wish.

If there is anyone who wishes to inherit the way of love by following the path of the one who is the master of love, if they say, "I will follow without carrying the cross," then they are all betrayers. Therefore, one must silently carry the cross and go over.

Even God rejected him. "Abba, Father, why have you forsaken me?" God also abandoned Jesus. Why did he abandon him? Did God send Jesus to die like that? God loved Jesus, but it was not God's wish for Jesus to die without being able to love even one person. Wouldn't that be the case? If God wanted him to die, what was the need to prepare for 4,000 years for Judaism and the Israelite people? He could have been born in a foreign land and died immediately...

God was astonished. "When I sent you, it was to be loved before the human world, yet you returned in such a ruined state..." Would God look upon that with approval? Is that God's will? The crosses of Christianity scattered throughout this world must be cut down and eliminated. The cross does not save. Because the cross came into existence, we cannot go the way of the cross without dying... It is a path of injustice and grievance.

Those who cannot empathize with the sorrowful heart of Jesus, who carried the cross toward Golgotha with a heart full of grievances and regrets, cannot enter into the authority of resurrection.

So who loved Jesus? Mary Magdalene loved Jesus. Then, how did Mary Magdalene love him? Did she try to love him from the position of being one with the heart of the Messiah, who bore the mission of the heavenly kingdom or the savior of the world? No. She loved him from a human perspective. Even if she wanted to represent her relatives, she could only wish to host Jesus on behalf of some Israelite, but she could not love him from the position of representing the church or the nation of Israel. Furthermore, she could not love him from the position of representing the world, saying, "I long for Jesus this much. I love him."

Look at the people Jesus faced. They were merely fishermen like Peter. He spoke of love to Peter, asking him three times, "Do you love me more than these?" Among the people Jesus faced was a woman named Mary, a widow with a difficult background. Then there was the Samaritan woman, who spoke so kindly at Jacob's well that even the disciples were suspicious. Who else was there?

He came to this earth as the protagonist of love—wasn't he the bridegroom and the protagonist of love? How could the group that appeared before the one who was the protagonist of love be so rough and unrefined? Was that what Jesus desired? No. Was that what God desired? No. Even the most miserable person seeks a good partner; no matter how poor a woman is, she seeks a good man as her husband. No matter how poor a man is, he seeks a good woman as his wife. Even those living under the power of death look for the opposite position, so how could Jesus, born as a prince of the heavenly kingdom, gather such utterly lowly fishermen and act as their leader? What did the group of prostitutes express as love? The Samaritan woman had five husbands; what does the Bible say about that? It is astonishing.

When Jesus asked the high priest of Israel, "Hey, do you love me more than these?" how wonderful it would have been to hear, "Yes, Lord, I have loved you." If Pilate had sent his attendants to come and say, "I have come to see you now," would God have felt displeased? Who would have thought it would end in such ruin?

Did God go through all that effort for 4,000 years to send the Messiah through the prophets just to let him perish? Being a prophet is not an easy task; they faced death and all kinds of sacrifices to lay the foundation for what would become customary. Did God pave the way for such a worthless, lonely death? Not a chance. You must understand that. Poor Jesus, poor Jesus.

What kind of parents did Jesus wish for? He should have been able to say to God, "My mother and father are the only ones in heaven and earth, so please love them more than me." Where did that hour of blessing go? When it came to his beloved siblings, he should have been able to say, "God, my beloved siblings are more precious than any siblings in heaven and earth. To be born as a human and have such siblings is a pride of heaven and humanity." Where was that moment of praise? Or when it came to his disciples, he should have been able to say, "I loved my disciples from a position of being the greatest teacher in the human world, with the authority to boast about them to the world, and I will love them." Where was that position? Centered around his clan, he should have been able to say, "My grandparents, or my distant relatives, our entire clan is a clan that heaven cannot help but love, and I cannot help but introduce them before you." Where was that joyful moment of introducing them to God and seeking God's blessing? It did not exist.
"Did you ever say, 'As you have walked the path of suffering for 4,000 years, enduring persecution from wicked groups and evil nations, I stand in a position to love this church and the nation of Israel that you wanted to love, so please accept this day as a day of fulfillment of wishes and love that you can rejoice in'? There was none. Not a single one.

From Jesus' perspective, it must have been astonishing when a lowly woman like Mary Magdalene came and poured perfume on His feet, wiping them with her hair. If He were like a worldly man, He might have kicked her away, but thankfully He did not. Even if a beautiful woman from a special priestly family had done that, it would have been bothersome, so what was that behavior? However, when Judas Iscariot saw that action and criticized it, Jesus could not help but side with her. 'She is better than you, Judas Iscariot. You harbor a treacherous heart that seeks my life, but that woman is better than you. How can you blame someone better than yourself?' He rebuked him.

We understand that the gospel only develops through the path of sacrificing one's entire self, and He even commanded, 'Wherever this gospel is preached, tell of her deed.' This is not because it is a good position. If Judas Iscariot had not acted that way, what would Jesus have done? He would not have said those words. You need to think about this.

Jesus came to spread the principles of love. He must love the nation, church, tribe, parents, and siblings that can be loved. First, centered on the nation that God has established, the center of that nation is the church, and the center of the church is the lineage of Joseph. The center of Joseph's lineage is the family of Joseph. The representative of Joseph's family is Mary. The central being that can come before Mary is Jesus.

Therefore, where does love begin? From Jesus, from Mary, from Joseph... There should be no trivial or frivolous siblings. There should not be any such siblings. Mary cannot be both the mother of Jesus and the mother of Satan. She should not become a mother who gave birth to a brother who opposes Jesus.

The nation that can embrace Eve is the nation of Adam. This is united, and within the realm of Satan, the Islamic realm of Barabbas and the communist world are connected. Therefore, we cannot leave the connection between Islam and the communist world as it is, which is why God has taken it away. 
Everyone, when looking at the current world situation, we cannot just stop because China or free China has calmed down. Because of that, significant issues will arise between the Soviet Union and China in the future. The United States must also reflect anew and find a way to unite the world, a way to receive support from the world. When this happens, a path will open for the Unification Church.

Because the Lord of heaven and earth has disappeared, a miserable fate has unfolded for all. We are now in that fate. A crossroads has formed between the communist realm and the democratic realm centered on the dividing line of left and right. There, the nation is being shattered into pieces. When you realize that, it is astonishing. If the Unification Church had not opposed it, Korea would not be like this today, and Christianity would not be like this. The man standing here speaking, if he had this much age, could have moved the world situation. Just yesterday, people from Japan came to ask me, "What will happen to Japan's situation in the future?" They created an environment where they could come to me, which is something that cannot even be dreamed of in the Republic of Korea. 
So, what kind of people will remain in the future? Those who are crazy for Jesus, those families that are crazy for Jesus, those churches that are crazy for Jesus will remain. The Unification Church says to be crazy for loving Jesus. They say that everyone goes crazy when they come to the Unification Church, right? That's good. It is a matter of life or death. When the husband dies and the wife collapses, isn't it a matter of life or death? What other wishes could there be? Our Unification Church is a matter of life or death. Do you understand? "Yes." 
Then, should we follow the path of the bridegroom or not? "We should follow." If a virgin's skirt is torn, should she follow even if she is in her underwear? Should she not follow? "Oh! How can I go when my skirt is torn and it's embarrassing? What if my pants are torn?" Look. To go to the Lord, if the skirt is torn, if the pants are torn, if one is naked and covered in blood, and collapses while going to the Lord, would the Lord see that and say, "Oh, well done! Since your strength is insufficient, that is your end"? The more miserable it is, the more it can become a motive to explode the bomb of love buried in the heart and to stimulate it. 
If the environment is difficult, the Lord would want to take on that difficulty with His body, and if He is wounded, wouldn't He bless it as a place where He can sympathize because He has taken on the trials of His own cross? Whether my body is torn or my reputation is trampled into the ground, that is not the problem. Those who care about their own conduct and reputation cannot go before God. 
By demonstrating the spirit of life or death, if mothers, brothers, and relatives had stood up against Pilate, or against the law scholars of that time, prepared for death, wouldn't there have been a riot? If there had been a riot, Jesus would not have died. 
Therefore, Unification Church members should go crazy. Who are they going crazy for? They must reject everything for the coming Lord. Those who think, "If I do this, I will meet the Lord and live well" cannot go to heaven. 
Where will the Lord take me when He meets me? He must lead the family, the tribe, the nation, the world, and pave the way of the cross. We must have a heart that can sympathize with that. That is why today, even the blessed families of the Unification Church are being chased out to the front lines.
