Now is not the time to live leisurely. 
That is why you are not in a situation to discuss anything now. You are not here to casually enjoy the breeze. You are here to fight to the death. Everyone, is that right? Would you rather die on Jesus' side, or would you rather die on the side of your husbands, your sons, and daughters? Ladies, which side would you die on? "On Jesus' side." You too? Would you rather die on the side of Jesus? How is it? "Oh, is it okay to die without even going to my in-laws?" What in-laws? What marriage? It means to throw it all away. Unless you become a foundation that can please God, you are bound to perish. 
The teacher has dedicated his whole life and walked the path of suffering and persecution because he knew that. "Let the wind blow. If the blowing wind goes away, it will go away, but I cannot be broken. Fierce storms, rage! I do not wish to turn back. I will go straight." Even though I have endured such fierce storms, I am still strong and capable. Some have fallen away while walking this path, but even while witnessing others falling, I did not sympathize with their falling and continued on. Thus, I have come this far. Many dropouts will occur from here as well. 
The question is, for whom do you move? Those who believe in the Unification Church for themselves will fall away. "I live for the world, and I live for my nation. I cannot live unless that nation lives, and I cannot live without a nation that fulfills the will of that world." One must have the heart that says, "Even if I die, I will go as quickly as possible to fulfill the will of that nation and that world." Only those who can do that will remain. If you seek only comfortable sleeping places, good food, and only places to rest comfortably, look at the year-round growth of a plant. It must grow in the same period as everything else until it sprouts leaves, blooms flowers, and bears fruit in the warm spring. If there is sap, it must absorb that sap and digest all the environmental conditions necessary for bearing fruit. Otherwise, no matter how lush the leaves and how beautiful the flowers are, it will not bear fruit. 
When we quietly observe the members of the Unification Church, we see some ladies who are very comfortable... that is not how it should be. They must be personal, familial, tribal, national, and global with the coming Lord.
We must pave the way to go to the world in alignment with the support. Wasn't that the path to take during Jesus' time? The same goes for you who have joined the Unification Church. You must love the church. How much should you love it? You must love it more than Jesus' relatives and kin. Do you understand what I mean? Without that love, you cannot enter heaven.

Do not think that this church exists to fulfill my will. This church exists to save the nation. It is absolutely not to send you out for the sake of the Unification Church. It is to send you out for the sake of the nation. When the nation stands before God's will, then it is not about saving the nation, but about going to save the world. We are looking for a nation that sacrifices for the world. You must understand that.

Those who wish to die for the nation live for the nation. When could Jesus love? When could Jesus sleep and rest in his parents' arms? When you think of Jesus, who could not have such things, you must have the heart that can rise up from your place and weep out loud, or else you cannot walk the path of the cross that Jesus left behind.

Where was the sovereignty that Jesus could love, the people that Jesus could love, the land that Jesus could love? It did not exist. The Israel that came to Jesus shed blood on the sovereignty, the nation, and the land, leaving behind the sad mark of death, didn't it? Then, there must be a nation here on this earth that can resurrect and achieve victory, and there must be a sovereignty and a land, right?

What kind of nation will that nation be? It will not be a glorious nation. Because it went through the cross, it must come through the cross. During Jesus' time, the nation that split around the cross with the thieves on the left and right must prepare a foundation to reunite in the future, and there is no other place in the world but Korea for that.

What is Panmunjom? It is the place where Satan and God accuse each other. It became Panmunjom because it could not become the Golden Gate. It is temporary, temporary. Satan and God are exactly the same. You should go to Panmunjom. It is like children fighting. Just like chicks fighting... There is only one such place on earth. That place is the barracks where Satan and God accuse each other. It is like the temple.

Just as Cain always struck first, we must go through the first, second, and third stages. We have come down to the second stage, right? Now we must determine the national fate at the third stage. The time has come to clash with the global fortune.

What will happen in the future? The Republic of Korea must unite around the path that heaven is taking. Now, it is a matter of whether we can or cannot do it. If we look for opposition parties, both will end up failing. The leaders are becoming busy. The Unification Church is also becoming busy. Because we stand at the forefront of the victory and anti-communist front, we have taken on the same fate. We have voluntarily stepped into the same fate. "Let us die for the nation." To die for the nation, we must love the nation even more.

Those who wish to die for the nation live for the nation. Isn't that right? Today, even if others flee, the members of the Unification Church will become the ones who protect this nation and uproot the last roots of communism. This is the resolve of the Teacher. That is why the Teacher wants to train you in military training. That is why I have created a gun factory. The pastors of established churches are still reporting to the government that the Unification Church is making guns. They say, "The Unification Church is a strong ideological organization and has a global foundation, so why doesn't the government let it be, as it could create a good opportunity for revolution by forming a political party?"

The problem is not Korea. The problem is not the president of Korea. The issue is the game of heaven and earth coming and going. The question is how to make this nation stand before God. What kind of president, what kind of political party? Political parties will all disappear in the end, later on. In the realm where Cain and Abel accuse each other...

The world we desire is not that kind of world. Is there democracy before God? Do you think democracy will last forever? Answer me. Is there democracy before God? If there is democracy before the Absolute Being, then there is no need for the noun "Absolute Being." The world of heaven is not a world of democracy. The world of democracy is where people buy and sell with money, where villains do all sorts of tricks to kill and save people, and where everyone is engaged in plundering wars to take away sovereignty.

What is the will? When we think about the path that Jesus must take centered on these issues, where have the true loving parents gone? Where have the brothers gone? We are saying we should take their place. How wonderful would it be if we could take the place of Jesus' parents and brothers? Let us set aside those flimsy Peter, James, and John, and all the apostles, and let us become the heads of the apostles, the apostles' leaders. Do you understand?

If a wife says, "Honey, the will is the will, but why are you leaving me behind?" when her husband is walking the path of the Unification Church, then she must be kicked aside and the path must be followed. Do you understand? You might feel bad hearing this, but... And the husband might say, "Oh, the will is the will, but isn't the husband the closest?" But what is close? Men are all thieves. They take things from the closest place. Isn't that right? That is why Jesus said, "Your household members are your enemies." In walking the heavenly path, that husband is a thief. Therefore, there is nothing to trust outside of the will.

What is the will? The other day, when a certain theology doctor came, our family asked, "What is God's will?" and he said, "It is an easy yet difficult question..." (laughter) A theology doctor who does not know God's will cannot do anything, and concludes it as something unknowable.

The Unification Church simply concludes what the will is. What is the will? It is to restore the world. What is the standard for restoring the world? It is to complete the ideal of creation. What is the ideal of creation? It is the completion of God's dual characteristics. It is clearly stated. To achieve that, it must go through the first, second, and third stages. That is why once you understand that, you will be busy.

That is why the founder of the Unification Church stands in a position where he is opposed by the nation, opposed by the denomination, opposed by the members, opposed by relatives, opposed by teachers, opposed by friends, and opposed by sons and daughters. In the end, he stands in a position saying, "Am I the only one left?"

Now we are going to rise up from the position of opposition. From the position of opposition, we will expand into what is good. If Korea opposes, it means that the will will be fulfilled in another country that is not Korea.

The Unification Church develops while being opposed. Christianity developed while being opposed, right? It is the same. Developing while being opposed is the work of the heavenly kingdom. Without opposition, there is no development. Why? Because the law of indemnity is established through the confrontation between Satan and God, there is no motivation for development without opposition.

That is why even if the Unification Church members say they are starving to death, they absolutely do not receive a single penny. While spending a lot of money on all sorts of entertainment elsewhere... Knowing the situation of hunger, they are told to love the nation. If you deviate from that, you will perish. Love the nation in difficult times, knowing that the heavenly kingdom is in a more urgent fate, endure that environment, and if you pass through that position, you will join the ranks of loyal patriots who have devoted themselves to the nation. This is the Unification thought. Moreover, this is the path that the members must take. I have walked that path.

Even when I was shackled and surrounded by enemies, I did not resent them. I still do. I pray, "God, let the enemies who imprisoned the founder of the Unification Church in jail be struck down by fire and annihilated." If I pray that three times, they will all fall into it. There is such a terrifying law.

Even without that, now everyone is raising their hands to perish. Isn't that right? Ordinary people are condemning the pastors of Christianity. "Pastor," with the character for "eye" (目) and "death" (死)... They are saying all sorts of things. That is how it is. But do not think that is good. Do you understand? If you laugh at the downfall and applaud, an arrow will fly back to you.

God says, "This is not because heaven is pleased. It is because there is a law, but if you are human, shouldn't you have affection? Shouldn't you show compassion?" When you execute your enemies, you should not turn around and say, "You bastard," but rather greet them and turn away. Do you understand what I mean? That is how it is. Even after crushing the enemy, you must turn around with respect.

He is in a solemn position where he sacrifices his life for the path he desires. Isn't that so? The claims and desired standards may differ, but the position where one can sacrifice their life, even if standing in an evil place, is precious.

As I mentioned before, I see the pastors holding public hearings, and when I look at them, I feel pity. I feel pity. I have been watching and listening, but I feel pity.

The path that the Unification Church must take. Therefore, you must know the path you must take in the future. We must follow the path that Jesus walked. Isn't that right? "Yes." That is why you must resolve the fact that Jesus could not have a mother he could love on this earth. You must become the ones who can love the kin that Jesus could not love. If you have a grandmother, love her like Jesus' grandmother; if you have a mother, love her like Jesus' mother; if you have siblings, you must create an environment where you can love them like the brothers Jesus would joyfully welcome.

Thus, you must dedicate your life for the kin, the nation, and the world that Jesus wanted to love. Because we know the path that Jesus took for that nation and world, we must be able to say, "I have loved," even if it means sacrificing our lives. If you die with the regret of wanting to come back, you cannot enter heaven. Do you understand?

The reason Jesus must come back is that he could only go to paradise and could not enter heaven. What kind of place is paradise? It is the waiting room to enter heaven. Therefore, unless you stand in a position where you can love the nation more than Jesus, you cannot resolve Jesus' resentment, and if you cannot resolve Jesus' resentment, you cannot fulfill the mission of the archangel. Men must fulfill the mission of the archangel, and then they must raise brides who can become Jesus' partners. That is why if you have daughters, you must love them in a way that carries on the tradition of loving heaven and the world. Without creating a kin that can make Jesus a son-in-law or establish a relationship with Jesus, you cannot become a member of the heavenly kingdom. Do you understand? This is what we, the Unification Church, want to do. Established churches cannot do it... That is why the term "family" was created.

Therefore, there are no distinctions between yellow, white, or black here. The world is one. Japanese people were enemies in the past, but once they enter the Unification Church, they become one. Japanese and Korean people marry each other. Germans and British people were enemies, but they marry each other. In the Unification Church, even in places where they do not speak the same language, they establish interpreters they desire and get married. Do you understand what I mean? Wouldn't it be fun for couples who love each other to have an interpreter? It is not that the founder of the Unification Church forces them to do this; they do it voluntarily. They have come to a time when they can do such things. It is good for Koreans to stick together. Therefore, it is not a matter of being good or bad. If you are a man, you are fine; if you are a woman, you are fine. (laughter)

Now, if Jesus, who came as a groom, could not have a day on this earth to fulfill his wishes by receiving a bride, wouldn't it be happiness for us today to resolve that and stand as attendants at Jesus' wedding banquet? Originally, it is not customary for unmarried men and women to be attendants. Nowadays, such people have emerged, but originally, attendants are exemplary couples who are married and living happily. Do you understand? So when Jesus comes to this earth to have a wedding banquet with a bride, if you can become a bride and groom who can stand as attendants, would you be unhappy or happy? The twelve disciples were established to create such attendants. When Jesus has a wedding banquet, all the attendants must celebrate.

In the Unification Church, there will be no other discussions in the future. If we talk centered around blessing, it will become a great topic. Let’s watch the recorded film of the blessing ceremony tonight. Cultural director, how did it go? "Yes, there are no problems." The part in Japanese didn't go well, did it? "Maybe one or two places..." When singing, the sound should come out, and you shouldn't just open your mouth. That is all. When singing, the song should come out, and it should be like that, but it has been cut off. "It was hard to match the mouth properly." That is what should be done, not that it is hard... When it is time to eat, you close your mouth, but you just have to move the spoon, right? (laughter) There were many places where Korean and Japanese were swapped... "If everyone comes tonight..." I cannot come because I have a meeting tonight. "Yes, I understand."

Let us resolve Jesus' resentment. Now, you must understand that you must resolve all the painful feelings and stories that Jesus could not achieve during his lifetime, the painful feelings of the only begotten son who received God's love, and today you must rise to that same emotional position and resolve it on this earth. There is a saying that shamans in the world perform exorcisms, right? If even evil spirits do that, then the good son of God, Jesus, must also perform that exorcism.

That is why, if you can be in a position where you can have parents who can do that on this earth, lead a kin that can do that, and lead a family that can do that, and if you can say, "Oh God, please love our kin, our denomination, our nation," then you will be able to stand in a position higher than what Jesus could achieve. Do you understand what I mean? In other words, unless you resolve what Jesus could not do, you cannot enter heaven.

It is not by faith that you are saved, but by love. Paul said that you are saved by faith, right? That means Paul did not understand well. You are saved by love.
he is. Do you understand? Jesus would want to save with love, wouldn’t He? He would want to save with faith, wouldn’t He? Jesus is the Jesus who loves faith, the Jesus who loves love, right? He loves faith, doesn’t He? In Christian terms, He is not the Jesus who loves love but the Jesus who loves faith. Therefore, it is said that you cannot be saved by love but only by faith.

Everyone, can you be saved by faith? If the bride believes in me well, is that good even if she doesn’t love me? (Laughter) Would you want to live like that? Would you want to live without love just because she believes in you day and night? Would you want to live by love or by faith? “By love.” Even if you ask kindergarten kids, they would say, “What kind of talk is that? How can you live by faith? You live by love.” Surely they would answer like that. You cannot be saved by faith.

You must love Jesus to the point of madness, to the point of your eyes falling out. You must love Him to the point of your eyes swelling with tears. Today, in this world, young men and women cherish their first love, but the love you must have is incomparable and cannot even be compared to that. You must have a heart that longs for God, to the point of shedding tears and snot, not caring about how your head looks or how your situation is. Is being in a position where you shed tears a bad position or a good position? The person in that position can meet someone, so there is a chance to meet, but those whose eyes are shiny and bright may not even meet at all. Even if they do meet, it would be uncomfortable. When the Lord comes, He will come in a pitiful state, having suffered and shed blood, looking terrible. Yet, despite that, they would be wearing fine clothes, smiling, and saying, “Oh, is He coming? Is He coming?” Think about it. If there were such a bride, would the men feel good? They would say, “What kind of strange girl is this?”

The Lord cannot come comfortably. Think about whether He would be comfortable. Consider how the Jesus who could not fulfill the will of love has suffered for thousands of years and how He would look when He comes.

So, when the Lord comes, He would instead say, “Hey, don’t cry. What is this? Why does your head look like this? Why do your clothes look like this? Why did you have to suffer so much to the point of being emaciated? Everything has become like this for me.” And if He were to give you back your head and your clothes, would that be glory or sorrow? “It’s glory.” It is indeed glory.

What would there be to comfort at the place where the Lord comes? What would there be to comfort in your situation? If this happens, the Lord, who has come with difficulty, will stand and comfort me, and that moment cannot be exchanged for anything in the world. The place where you can comfort others is indeed a happy place. Do you understand?

That is why it is said that those who endure to the end will be saved. What do they have? Is it faith that endures to the end? Those who endure to the end have love. What do they have? “Love.” You know that. It is those who endure to the end with love who will be saved. You cannot be saved by faith. Faith is only a guiding role. It is a guide to this threshold. Faith is like taking the bride to the bridal chamber and saying, “That man is your husband.” After that, the living is not done by faith. What is it done by? It is done by love.

Now that the end has come, the era of faith is passing, and it is time to prepare the bride adorned with love, to shine her integrity and chastity in all environments of life. Let us prepare to present a new bouquet to the world Christian community and to the coming Lord. If we cannot have a bouquet, let our bodies become a fragrant bouquet, and let our organization be offered as a bouquet. Do you understand?

We must become flowers that can emit fragrance. What does that mean? It means we should become a form that the Lord can come to and feel compassion for and rejoice in. That place is not a place of laughter and dancing. You must understand that.

If you become someone who keeps that path and follows that path, you will undoubtedly become a companion on the path that Jesus must take and an heir of God’s love. I hope you remember this as I share these words.

<Prayer> Father, as the Unification Church has come this far, please take the place you dislike and with the resentment that pierces your heart, may you admonish us.

We have come this far while fighting to surpass the final peak you have commanded. Now, on the global trend advancing toward the 7/8/9 peaks, Father, have compassion on us.

We must not inherit the peak of the cross filled with sorrow, despair, sighs, and groans. We have realized that today, the Unification Church is on the path that can inherit hope, resurrection, and victory.

Father, when we think about it, it has been a tedious path. When we think about it, it has been a remarkable path. When we think about it, there have been many stories we could not bear to walk. However, we know that the stories of heaven are greater than the stories of those on earth, so even if it is a path that could lead to ruin, we have followed it because it is the path you walk. As we followed it, when we think about the group that was supposed to perish but is standing in a place that does not perish, we cannot help but bow down and give thanks every time we realize that this is not anyone’s merit but the result of your blood, tears, and sacrifice.

If there are sons and daughters who spend the night crying out to you as their Father, you must not say you do not know. Please be with them forever.

We know that in the path of Jesus, who came to this earth and lived for over 30 years, you were there, and every time He prayed through the night on the Mount of Gethsemane, you were there, revealing the future stories. We ask once again that the heavenly counsel from that deep place never leave us.

Father, this place is not anyone’s place. What this son desires is how to develop the pioneering path for the nation you desire into a glorious traditional path, and I am trying to keep this place with the same concern you have. I believe you know this.

Please lead us to a result that can be suitable before your will as we walk this path. If we stand in a position that is not suitable, Father, please discipline us so that we can always hold onto a position that is suitable before you, and may we not become a group that has abandoned heaven and left heaven. I earnestly ask you to guide us.

We have realized that before that nation perishes, that tribe must perish, and before that tribe perishes, that family must perish. We have realized that before that family perishes, we as individuals must perish. Jesus came to seek not individuals but families. The path that families must take is for the sake of the tribe, so families must sacrifice to seek the tribe. To seek the nation, the tribe must sacrifice. To seek the world, the nation must sacrifice.

Today, when we see that there is no nation that sacrifices for the world, we can surely conclude that this is an evil world, so we earnestly ask that the Unification Church members do not delay in preparing for the fight to establish a national sovereignty that can sacrifice for the world.

If there is a group that possesses such ideological determination and puts forth all their intellect, that group will not perish but will dominate history and can establish a holy nation and a holy people that will leave a new traditional culture in the history of the universe. I earnestly ask that you allow us to be a group that fights until the end and remains to comfort you in that place and to praise your glory.

Please remember this day. May all the stories up to October of this year be concluded as your satisfaction, and may we, through the remaining two months, once again reorganize and settle, allowing this understanding to become a year of victory and a year of praise before the nation and heaven.

Please personally oversee and guide the entirety of today. Over your children scattered throughout South Korea and the world, and over the many brothers centered around the churches, may you extend your infinite mercy and love so that the days of victory may unfold quickly before them.

I earnestly ask that the grace and blessing of eternal longevity be with those who are determined to walk the path of sacrifice for your will. I pray this in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

3) Practitioners of Unification Thought
Whether you eat barley rice or live in a shabby room, that is not the issue. If you have poured everything into trying to settle that environment without caring about all the hardships and died in the process, it is not that you died because your life was over, but if you died at the hands of the enemy, would people say, “That person died well”? The question is whether that person died for themselves or for others. If they died fighting for the whole, the more miserable the content of that struggle, the more their name shines. Isn’t that right? 

People who live for others receive the admiration of many.
Everyone has a desire to live well. However, if there is a king who thinks, “What’s the point? I’ll just live moderately; what does it matter if I make the people suffer a bit for my own good?” the entire nation would expel that king. 

If a king who worked only for his own glory died, the people would say he died well, but if there is a king who sacrificed for the glory of the whole, wouldn’t people want to leave that king’s name in history forever? Isn’t that right? 

On November 6, 1971, in the evening, at Gwangju Church.
* This message was given at a special meeting attended by members from Jeollanam-do and Jeollabuk-do before the third tour, and the recording was provided by Chairman Roh Eung-kyu of Hyunbomun Church, although the beginning part was not recorded. The title was added by the editor.

If you live for yourself and die, your name disappears. There is nothing left. However, if you live for others and die, do you leave a legacy or not? If the foundation where you lived for others was the village, the village head or concerned individuals would hold a memorial service on the day of your death. If someone died for the county, the county residents would come together to hold a memorial service. If someone died for Jeollanam-do, the dignitaries of Jeollanam-do would come together to hold a memorial service.

What do people do during the memorial service? They pledge to inherit the thoughts and all the public deeds left by that person, hoping to align themselves ideologically and practically with that person’s life and struggles. Isn’t that right?

If there is someone who sacrificed for the whole of South Korea, and even more so, if there is someone who sacrificed more than the president of South Korea… When comparing a president who lived for his own pleasure with an ordinary citizen who dedicated their life for the happiness of the entire nation, even if they lived in the same era, the name of the president who lived for himself will not remain, but the name of the person who lived for the glory of the whole will remain. If there are 30 million people, they should all come together to remember that person. That is undeniable, right? 

Just like the athletes who participated in a marathon, if they took a break for about five minutes focusing on themselves, that would end as a self-centered break, but if they took a break for five minutes for others, that will shine brightly in history. That is for sure. Do you understand? 

You might think, “That sounds unpleasant. Why live for others?” But historically, the materials of those who lived for others are collected and preserved, while those who lived for themselves, no matter how much material they have, are discarded. History has been like that, hasn’t it? 

People who live for themselves versus those who live for others.
Imagine someone in the neighborhood who works day and night for themselves. Nowadays, what time does the sun rise? It rises after five, before six, right? The sun rises before six, but that person wakes up at four and makes noise and busies themselves working for themselves while others are still asleep. Even at midnight, they work without rest, barely saving money to live comfortably. It is said that because that person lived like that all their life, they have a house now, and nowadays they probably have a car, and a few sacks of rice in their storage. Everything seems to be in order.

However, there is another person in that neighborhood who does not take care of their own home. They do not think about their spouse or children; they only wake up to serve others. They wake up early in the morning to do good deeds not just for their neighborhood but for the entire town and county. They spend their whole life like this, and in the end...
Let's say he played around while getting meals. For example, that's how it turned out.

Having served throughout his life, he has not a penny in his pocket, nor a single handkerchief left. I have a nice handkerchief, you know. When I try to take out my wallet, my hand comes out through my pocket without any resistance. (Laughter) Not only that, but in the summer, I should be wearing summer clothes, yet I'm living in padded clothes. I have no clothes. Can you choose what you get to wear? In winter, I should be wearing padded clothes, but I'm wearing summer clothes. Do you all want that?

Those who came here today might think, "He only says unpleasant things," but please don't think too harshly. That would be disappointing. (Laughter) 

When I die after living like this, my wife or children won't have a bowl to serve rice in. There will be just one broken bowl left and a spoon that is already broken and waiting to break even more. Even if there isn't such a spoon, it means that I used everything up, eating and cleaning it all. 

When there are these two types of people, who would you follow? Would you follow someone who left at least a room behind after living like that, or someone who ended up in ruin? Which person would you follow? Answer clearly. Let’s move on after you answer. Isn't that right, everyone? Treating guests well brings blessings. So, which person would you follow? You might think, "Why is he asking such difficult questions?" but that's what makes it interesting. (Laughter) You might be too grown up to get many points for this, but have you thought about how elementary school kids or kindergarten children would answer this?

When comparing a person who lived their whole life without thinking of themselves and died for others, and someone who lived only for themselves, which person is better? The one who lived for others is in a terrible situation. That's something no one wants to even think about. You would feel the same.

However, if you ask elementary school students or kindergarten children who a great person is, they would say it’s someone who helps others. Why is it that living for oneself doesn't make one a great person? Don't they eat well, wear good clothes, and live well? Aren't they not hungry, sleeping in a warm room in winter and going to cool places in summer? Why is that?

Why does history consider later people to be greater than earlier ones? That is an undeniable fact. Is there anyone who disagrees? Raise your hand if you think that statement is wrong. Those who raise their hands should be beaten up. (Laughter) You all know that, right? Isn't that true? "Yes."

Ah! What on earth has happened in this world? What kind of game is this? There are two types of people: those who lived well for themselves and those who lived poorly and died. The standards are different. The latter's purpose is for the whole, while the former's is for themselves. That is the difference.

Then, who are the saints and sages in history? That's the question. If I keep talking like this, time will pass quickly. Should I make it shorter or longer? "Make it longer." I find it tiring, and many of you sitting for a long time must be feeling uncomfortable, right? "No, I'm not." It’s hard to sympathize with those who are struggling, so it’s reasonable to shorten the time, right? (Laughter) Isn’t that so? "No." Really? "Yes." If I make my speech shorter, those standing here would be happy. I'm starting to sweat now. Many people are struggling, and it's hard for me too, so is there really a need to do this? "It should be fine." Do you want that or not? "I don't want that." You don’t want it? "No." Even though it’s hard, you don’t want it? "Yes." That’s strange. Why would you want something that’s hard? "There’s a lot to gain." There’s a lot to gain? "Yes." What will you do with what you gain? If you become skilled and turn into a thief or a con artist, what will happen? (Laughter) Is that why? If so, I shouldn’t even appear at all. Whenever someone comes out and speaks, someone from our neighborhood would say, "What’s wrong with that person?" (The recording cuts off briefly.)

The value of the same action changes based on the motivation behind it.

So, is there a good person and a bad person? If everyone here is labeled as a bad person, it would feel unpleasant. When you see someone with wide-open eyes, they might seem good, but I mentioned earlier that there might not be truly good people. So, if the governors of Jeollanam-do and Jeollabuk-do agree to select a representative person for Jeollanam-do, can that person be the best in South Korea? They can compete with representatives from other provinces, right? Do you know what that means? It means they could be a loser. Isn’t that so? They could be a loser.

Then, can the best person in South Korea be the best in the world? Is that possible or not? It’s not that it’s entirely impossible. There’s a possibility of being the best, but you won’t know until you try. To be the best, what should you do? If the average person in the world is this thick, then a person selected from South Korea only needs to be one layer thicker than that person to be the best, right? "Yes." Even if it’s not a layer but just a single piece of paper thicker, that person is the best, right? If it’s just one hundredth of a piece of paper thicker, that person is still the best, right? "Yes." That’s how it is.

So, how much difference is there between the first and second place? There’s almost none. Nowadays, isn’t that right? When playing baseball, if they can’t distinguish between an out and a safe, they record the scene at high speed and check it within a fraction of a second. That’s how they determine first and second place. If someone ends up in second place like that, would they feel good or bad? If they didn’t win on the world stage, it would be frustrating, right?

What’s the reason they didn’t win? If during practice, a friend comes and says, "Hey, let’s go, something good is happening today," and they think, "What’s wrong with listening to friends?" and go, then they might end up in second place because they couldn’t practice for a day. Isn’t that right? Just one day without practice can lead to a thousand years of regret. It’s not just one day; even one hour or one moment of mistake can ruin a thousand years of history.

You know, if you go to prison, the teacher has experience. They’ve been in and out of prison and have been doing this kind of thing until now. When you enter prison, no one thinks, "I’m going to prison." Do you think there are people who would act that way? If you think about going to prison, would you do such things? If you know how terrible prison is, would you? No, right? "Yes." No one thinks, "I’m going to prison."

If you look into the motivation for entering prison, there’s not a single person who planned it from the womb. They just happened to meet a friend on the market street, and the friend said, "Hey, if you do this, you’ll be fine. Just listen to me, and you can live comfortably for the rest of your life." So, they thought, "Really? Let’s give it a try." That’s how greedy groups end up in prison. 

With just one word, they start following that path step by step.

In doing so, they ruin their whole family, ruin themselves, and ruin their wife and children. They end up sitting in prison, saying, "Oh," and regretting it. I’ve seen many people sighing alone. When they think about it, it’s shocking. "If I hadn’t moved at that moment, I wouldn’t have committed a crime. Oh, that moment is the problem…" I’ve seen many people groaning like that. Therefore, the motivation for rise and fall is not based on thousands of years; it is determined in a moment. That’s how it is. Do you understand? "Yes."

It is determined in a moment, but if there is someone who has acted for others in the same event, their thoughts are fundamentally different from someone who acted purely to satisfy their own desires.

For example, let’s think about an orphanage director. This director is someone who takes care of hundreds of children, feeding and clothing them, but as winter approaches and there are no clothes to dress them in, if they get caught up in a situation because they thought it was a good idea, then the content is different, and so is the outcome.

When they go to court to be judged, a person who committed a crime for their own desires has a path that can be criticized by anyone, and because they have that potential, there’s no room for sympathy. However, in the case of the orphanage director, their path is not for their own desires but from the standpoint of being responsible for the lives of those hundreds of children. They were struggling to prepare clothes for the upcoming winter, and they didn’t know it would end up like this when they trusted a friend and stepped out. So, what will the judge’s ruling be? Even if both people end up in the same situation, one person will receive a sentence that cannot be forgiven, while the other will be emphasized as "this person is a victim of good intentions, and there should be many people like them among our citizens," and they will be acquitted. 

If the judge made such a ruling, would the audience of 500, 50,000, 500,000, or 50 million people shout, "Beat that judge, kill him!"? Rather, the audience would feel pity. When they hear his testimony, they cannot help but sympathize. If the audience hoped to save that person and then heard such a ruling, everyone would be happy. Isn’t that so? This is the kind of result that occurs.

When you see this, why do the masses want to support that person? Why do they hope for that person’s future? Why do they want to stand in the position of that person’s defense attorney? Where does that reason lie? If you deny it, the path of history will be broken, and the good actions that humanity desires will come to an end, falling into a trap and descending into the world of death. Our conscience knows this implicitly, which is why we want to stand on that side. This is because everyone has the inherent action of pursuing such things, and it is undeniable that this leads to such results. Do you understand? "Yes."

God rewards those who seek to help others.

Everyone attending this gathering must have thought, "Since the teacher is coming to Gwangju today, I should go." "The teacher is coming, so I should go. As a member of the Unification Church, I must go. But how do I get there? Is there a car available?" Is there a car here or not? This is a one-way road, so there’s no way to come and go, right? "I shouldn’t just take any car; I should take the best car and enjoy a nice meal at a restaurant on the way." Let’s say someone came with that mindset.

On the other hand, there are those who, upon hearing the teacher is coming to Gwangju, couldn’t sleep at night, and there are people who have only one set of clothes, and selling it wouldn’t even cover half the fare, so they went out to work hard to earn the fare. There are those who, having not a single penny, sweat and labor to prepare the fare to come here.

Also, when the mother says she will go, perhaps the children or even the husband say, "You go, mother. Please come back." There are families that come together to send their mother off with all their efforts. There might also be a church that, since not everyone can go, decides to send at least one person, and the whole church unites to send that one person.

So, among the 500 people here, each person’s background and circumstances are all different.

When coming here, some might arrive in the best car, enjoying gourmet meals, and as soon as they arrive at Gwangju Station, they take a taxi to the Gwangju Church, sitting at the front to see every detail of the teacher’s face… (Laughter) Why are you laughing? (Laughter) People need stimulation, so I make expressions to leave an impression on you. Don’t forget that. Even if it’s unpleasant, I can’t help but make such impressions. Do you understand? "Yes." Not everyone sitting here is like that. They might be, but that’s not what I’m saying. (Laughter)

Now, there are those who, feeling anxious because it’s getting late, rush to catch a taxi, saying, "Oh, what time is it? Hurry up, hurry!" and while fighting with the driver, they might hear the driver complain, "This country woman is probably coming to Gwangju for the first time, why is she in such a hurry? Oh, how unpleasant." 

Now, if that’s the case, did they do something good or bad to the driver on the way? They made the driver feel bad all day, so was it a good thing or a bad thing? In a one-on-one situation, it’s a bad thing. However, what is my purpose in going? "I came here representing my husband, my children, and my church. I can’t miss even one word from the very first moment. I need to see the teacher’s expression and report back, so I can’t afford to be late." If I had that mindset and urged the driver, did I do well or poorly? "You did well." Really? "Yes." I’m not sure. No matter how I think about it, I’m not sure. (Laughter)

If I did it for myself, that would be bad. If a young woman goes to hear the teachings and has a chance to meet a good husband, that would be a failing grade. If I’m going for the sake of the whole, for others… In such cases, it’s not a sin to look down on those who don’t act for others. Do you understand? Even if it causes some pain, there is a way to escape. You know that, right? "Yes."

So, when we say God knows everything, which person will He choose as the best? "Oh, I’m a former governor." Or, "I have experience as a department head. Still, I’m someone who responds when called." If someone like that thinks, "What is this Unification Church leader talking about?" there could be all kinds of people, about 500 different situations. 

On the other hand, there might be someone who thinks, "How rewarding it is to have worked my whole life for this day! I wish I had worked a little harder." They might be crying and sobbing. It’s the complete opposite.

When there are these two types of people, if God were to score them, which side would He give a higher score? What do you think? If that’s the case, wouldn’t you feel out of place? Isn’t that right? If God gives the first place, the best…
A person who has come up from a miserable position while working hard, someone who represents not just their personal circumstances but the overall situation with a heartbreaking story, is the one who should be given first place. The more they are in an environment where they forget their own existence in front of that situation and could collapse, the more they deserve to be recognized. Is that right or not? "That's right." Without such a person, it would be impossible to give first place to anyone else. If I were to give first place to someone else, if God had a collar, I would pull on it. I would say, "Hey, hey." Then God would respond, "This guy?" At that moment, I could even speak informally, saying, "What's going on?" In such cases, it wouldn't be a problem to do so.

If such a person exists, are they standing in a public position or a private one? The one who says "What's going on?" is someone who wants to establish a public position by justly judging the situation, and therefore, God would not say, "Hey, you fool. I lost. You foolish child," but rather should commend that person. Shouldn't it be so?

Now, listening to what the teacher said, the more someone has suffered, the higher their score? "Higher." Yes, indeed. Even when viewed from a personal perspective, those who have suffered have a higher score, and the broader their heart for others and for the whole, the more their score increases. Do you understand? That is a leap. It is a jump. You all need to understand this.

History unfolds in this way, and the distinction between good and evil is established and set through such environments in our living conditions, a fact we cannot deny in our emotional experiences or environments. You must clearly understand that these stories are intertwined.

Everyone wants to be a good person, but it requires a lot of effort. Earlier, we talked about good and bad people. Raise your hand if you want to be a bad person. Would anyone raise their hand if I said, "I'm dying, and since you aren't raising your hands, I'm going to die. Raise your hand"? If I asked for people who want to be bad and no one raised their hand, would I die because of that? In such a case, it is something you should not raise your hand for even if you die. Right? Would you raise your hand or not? "I wouldn't." You are heartless. (Laughter) It's okay to be heartless. I don't feel bad about it. That's how it should be. That heartlessness is what I welcome.

When I say, "Raise your hand if you want to be a good person," no one would refrain from raising their hand, right? Looking closely, everyone seems to be ready to raise their hands. They think that the teacher will ask them to raise their hands, so they are all prepared. There is no need to ask. No one wants to be a bad person. Everyone wants to be good, right? "Yes."

Everyone wants to be good, but have they become good or not? Have they become good or not? "Not yet." Why haven't they become good? That's why they are trying again. Even if a bad person doesn't want to be bad, what happens? They become bad without even thinking about it. A bad person doesn't even need to think. Even if they hear such words and go out, if they see a lady with a baby and say, "What is this?" and hit her, that person is a bad person, right? What kind of thought is that? In an instant, they become a bad person. However, can a good person become good in an instant? "No." Goodness does not happen in an instant.

Evil is determined, judged, and acted upon in an instant. However, goodness is not like that. Goodness does not happen in an instant. There is no way for something true to come into being without roots or foundations in an instant. Evil can arise without roots or foundations. Isn't that right? If you rush, it is evil. Isn't that so? Evil can happen in an instant without roots or foundations, but goodness cannot happen without roots or foundations. A person who hopes for goodness does not become good temporarily. That is proven by history. You must create connections centered around your life in all directions.

When you look ahead and encounter obstacles, as long as you are blocked, it is good. Do you understand? Then, when you look back, if you are blocked, it is good to the extent that you are blocked. If you look ahead and are never blocked, does that feel good or not? "It feels good." If you look back and are never blocked, does that feel good or not? "It feels good." Then, if you look left and right and are never blocked, that is also good. If you look up and down and are never blocked, that position is also good. Do you want that or not? "We want it." Oh, how exciting would that be?

You must understand well. Goodness does not happen in an instant. To become a good person, you must inherit from the past. That is why education is necessary. Isn't that so? You need to go to school and learn. What do you learn? Historically, those who sacrificed to pave the way for goodness did not live well and die. Therefore, you must inherit the historical thoughts of those who sacrificed.

Then, who is a patriot in the Republic of Korea? A loyal subject cannot exist while alive. Do you understand? One cannot be a loyal subject before dying. Some might say, "You can be a loyal subject while alive, not just after dying," but that is a million miles off. Let's say there are about a hundred loyal subjects. Among them, there may be one who is the absolute worst, someone who has no history of being a loyal subject, just a weakling. But during a time of national emergency, when a hundred loyal subjects fight for the country, that utterly useless loyal subject dies in that war. After that person dies, let’s say the war is won. Of course, all one hundred loyal subjects participated, and others may have achieved many merits in battle, but in that war, the most loyal subject is the one who sacrificed their life, surpassing the other ninety-nine loyal subjects. Even if someone contributed money and dedicated their life, if they did not sacrifice their life, can they stand in front of the one who did? "No." You understand that well. They cannot.

The level of sacrifice in giving one's life is determined by how miserable that sacrifice was. If three people die together, one dies from a stray bullet, another is stabbed hundreds of times in battle, and the third fights at the front lines, gets captured, has their ears cut off, eyes gouged out, nose torn, tongue cut, fingers severed, limbs amputated, and ends up as a mangled body dragged around until they eventually die as dog food, who among the one shot, the one stabbed, and the one who died as dog food is the top loyal subject? (Laughter) While such cases may not exist, the more extreme and miserable the situation, the more value it has, right? "Yes." Is that really true? "Yes." You are learning from me. Is that really true? "Yes." Really? "Yes." You all know this, but you thought only I knew. (Laughter) That is why education is necessary.

Now, let’s say the loyal subject who died as dog food says, "Oh, I can't do this. I'm dying. Your Majesty, are you going to let me die like this without helping me?" If they die like that, can they be called a loyal subject? Can they be? "No." When the truth is revealed, they will be called, "This guy, a horrible person, trying to tarnish the history of loyal subjects and steal the altar of sacrifice." You all need to understand this. "I didn't realize that coming to this assembly would lead to such a dramatic outcome."

However, if someone, centered on the king they serve, says, "Instead of my arm being torn, my arm should be torn; instead of their eyes being gouged out, my eyes should be gouged out; instead of their miserable death, I should die," and dies with the hope that "I hope the day will come when I can be a sacrifice for the king's liberation," then if God exists, He will know this situation and will count that person among the first of the loyal subjects who shine for eternity. Such a person is more than qualified to be a loyal subject.

If there is a loyal subject who died like that, then no matter how fierce the wars that follow, those who fall in battle cannot show their faces in front of that loyal subject. They can eternally hold the rank of the top loyal subject. With the thought of being the foremost ideology to serve the king and being a sacrifice for the people governed by the king, if they die without a speck of dust or a hair's breadth of selfishness, their loyalty will be remembered even if that history disappears. Even in other countries, that spirit will be inherited as the spirit of their nation. That is how such nations arise. Do you understand? This is astonishing.

Then, what kind of person can be a global figure? Who can win on a global scale? It is someone who stands at the peak of overcoming extreme suffering for their country and who does not bend their beliefs, walking unilaterally on principled standards. Do you like unilateral paths? Is there anyone who likes unilateral paths? When you take a taxi and are in a hurry, if you can get there quickly, but there’s a sign saying "One-way," does that make you feel good? In such cases, if we were members of the Unification Church, we would say, "Oh, you devil!" (Laughter) That means it feels bad. However, a person who walks a unilateral path, not a four-way path, will be remembered in history and can easily join the ranks of saints, and you need to understand that.

What is good and what is evil? When we look at it this way, we must understand what is good and what is evil. What is evil? We need to understand this. Evil is nothing other than trying to establish oneself and subjugate the world. It is disregarding the principles of heaven and earth, denying all reason, and rejecting all public laws of society, thinking, "I will do whatever I want in this world." A being born with a fleeting life does not know the past, does not know the present, does not know the future, and only thinks, "As long as I do well."

When we look at the long history of humanity, a human life is but a fleeting moment. It is fleeting, right? "Yes." With such a fleeting and short life, there are those who say, "I will do as I please, regardless of God or saints. My fist is the strongest." They do not even know their parents. Human judgment is received both in life and after death. It is received in life and after death.

In comparison to eternity, life is but a fleeting moment. "I was born to live well... I am the best." There are many young people like that these days. I hope no one like that is here, but I want to believe there is no one like that. However, there might be someone who has thought that way. Isn't that right? Because they have come into the Unification Church, they have changed, but I know there are people like that. "I only have my fist. What is God? What are the president and the country? In Jeonju and Gwangju, I am the best. If I swing my fist, I will get immediate results. Even when I am hungry, if I shout once, food will come flying." That feels good, doesn't it? Well, it does feel good, right? What happens to such people?

Those who pursue immediate action and immediate enjoyment are evil people. Goodness does not manifest immediately. Do you understand? You need to understand this. Goodness has history. Goodness has righteousness. Because there is righteousness, it represents the times. There is a future. You should not lean towards history; you must inherit the public lives of many historical figures who have passed.

What kind of lives did great people live? There has never been a great person who sacrificed their life for themselves. Has anyone become great by being stabbed while trying to knock someone down? Only those who sacrifice their lives for the whole, such as the nation or the people, can become great. Such people become the foundation of history and contribute to its elevation through that history.

While living a public life, those who consider public sacrifice and public destruction as glory and endure it themselves, saying, "I will be sacrificed, but the world I desire will surely be realized after this time," are the ones who can become patriots when they stand in a national position and can become great people. When they stand in a global position, they can surpass being great and become saints.

A saint is a global person. They do not only love their nation but love all humanity. They do not only love the present but love the future and eternity. They live in the present position that everyone has demanded, as the embodiment of desires from the past.

In living, those who reject the notion of wanting to live well for themselves from the beginning and have the idea of sacrificing infinitely, saying, "I will sacrifice myself so that the whole can do well," are the saints who remain in history. There is no saint who is not a global person.

How many saints are there? Try calling them out. "Jesus." The members of the Unification Church do not start by calling out Jesus. They should think of others first. (Laughter) Have you been listening until now? If you have listened, you should know how to respond. Jesus is a saint, but if he has righteousness and thinks of the future...

When there is a feast in the neighborhood, the groom should treat the beggars well before he comes to receive the feast. What happens if the groom makes a fuss when it's time to receive the feast? If he says, "The owner didn't give me even one rice cake, so please give me one," who can say anything about that? Then it would be a big deal. Right? "Oh, what a disgrace to the family," or "Oh, what a mistake in marrying." Even if the bride is beautiful, they would say, "Oh, what a mistake." If a man with a purpose were to say, "This is going to be a big deal," then it would be a big deal, so on the day of the feast, they must treat the beggars well. Do you understand? "Yes." Unification Church members should know this.

However, when it comes to a joint wedding ceremony, there may not be anything for the beggars to eat, right? (Laughter)
When you have a wedding reception, you should at least bring a bag of snacks and say, "I'm sorry that we don't have anything to eat since you all came to see our celebration today." Then, from your nice suit pocket or from the bride's side, you should take out the snack bag and offer it to them. Although this joint wedding ceremony seems nice, there might be some disappointment, so you should say, "Please have one." Then God will see and say, "Today, among all the blessed grooms and brides, you are the best." Isn't that right? "That's right." You need to understand these things.

How many saints are there? When you call their names, you should know them all. In a gathering of about 500 parents, when asking the students, "Whose parents are the best?" if they say, "Our mom and dad," then it means, "That kid only knows his own parents." In that case, what should they say? They should say, "All parents are good, but our mom and dad are the best." Then people will think, "Oh, that kid is something." Isn't that right? That's how it should be. So, who is a saint? (Laughter) Are you embarrassed? Then I'll call them out for you. Buddha, Confucius, "Socrates," Socrates? "Muhammad," Muhammad, and then who? "Jesus." Jesus has become a bit of a joke. (Laughter) It's not a joke to say it later.

Even if a friend comes, even if they are the class president or an honor student, they shouldn't say, "Hey, since you came, do me a favor." When a friend comes, they should say, "Come in, come in. I'm usually good at this. I'm having a meal now, so sit here." They should offer the meal and do favors for them. Then later, the other friends will think, "That friend is really nice." Right? But if someone is wealthy, they shouldn't say, "Hey, maid, maid! Our friend is here. Bring some rice cakes." That shouldn't happen. (Laughter) When you see things like that, you should understand that in all aspects of social life, good and evil are intertwined. You need to understand why I'm saying this.

Now, as I mentioned earlier, there are Muhammad and Socrates, but can Socrates be considered a saint? Socrates cannot be included. The Mission of the Evangelist and the Heart of Heaven

The church leaders are going out to evangelize, and whether or not evangelism is successful is the most important issue. You are meeting people, but if they do not move, and even if you speak, the listeners do not feel touched, this must be the most burdensome issue for you.

People of the satanic realm, people of the intermediate realm, people of the heavenly realm.

In the fallen world, there are people in the realm of satan, the realm of satan. Beginners may not understand this well, but there are people in the realm of satan. Then there are people in the intermediate realm between the satanic and heavenly realms. And there are also people who are not in the satanic realm or the intermediate realm but are within the heavenly realm. Generally, we can divide people into these three categories.

If we center on the individual, there is the body and the mind. Here, the mind is neither of the body nor of the spirit. It is intermediate, like space. So, there are physical people, mental people, and then there are spiritual people.

In the same way, there are people on the side of the satanic world, then there are people in the intermediate layer, and then there are people on the side of heaven.

The reason some people feel good when they meet someone.

When we look at people, it may differ from individual to individual, but some people just feel good when we meet them. Even if it is the first time meeting that person, there is a natural attraction. Why is that? It is because that person has a higher spiritual standard than oneself. When that person is at a higher standard than what one’s ancestors have established, it naturally feels good when we meet them. This is because if a connection is established with that person, it will not be a loss for us but a benefit.

Whether a person is good or bad is determined by whether the relationship leads to a loss or a gain. Everyone dislikes what is bad and likes what is good.

There are also people who are neither good nor bad. Such people exist. Then there are those who, for some reason, seem unpleasant. This is how it is. There are people who feel good when we meet them, there are those who are just okay, and there are those who, for some reason, we just dislike. This feeling arises because the counterpart transmits some kind of wavelength like a signal.

From that perspective, you must analyze well. When you feel good about someone, it means that, in principle, they have become the subject and you are in the position of the object, exchanging with them. If you think centered on the principle, you will understand that when a perfect reciprocal standard is established and a perfect reciprocal expectation is achieved, God’s presence is there. This is the teaching of the principle.

In the same way, when you feel good about someone, even if you are in an undesirable environment, there is something about them that makes it impossible for you not to give, and you find yourself in a position where you cannot help but receive from them. In other words, if there is a strong magnet and iron, the iron is influenced by the magnet. Isn’t that so? When influenced, the iron itself is inevitably drawn to it. Because of this kind of interaction, even if it is not visible to your eyes, an unseen bond is formed between the two. Therefore, the greater the bond of giving and receiving, the more God’s presence will be there.

As much as the power of giving and receiving corresponds, movement will occur, and it will inevitably move while seeking a center. When there is giving and receiving, movement occurs. When movement occurs, it will always seek a center. If the center is determined quickly, it will continue for a long time, but if the center is not determined for a long time and is slower than the giving and receiving, it will collapse quickly. This is how it is.

When there is giving and receiving, God will surely be present, and the center will be determined. We have learned this from the principle, so there are people who feel good from the very beginning. There is a feeling of goodness for some reason. There is definitely a connection here. Even though you may have just met, you are now separated by surnames like Park, Kim, Choi, Jo, Moon, and others, but there was a connection among your ancestors.

If you investigate our past ancestors, there were grandmothers of the Jo family, grandmothers of the Kim family, and if you look at all the grandmothers who married into different families, you will see that many surnames have come together and separated. The grandmother of the Choi family came and left, and the grandmother of the Kim family came and left. If you trace back through your ancestors, you can see that many clans have come together and separated from one grandfather to the present father’s generation. One life passes, and another life passes, and this is how it is.

As this continues, in proportion, there is a specific surname centered around one’s own lineage or clan. Among your grandmothers, which surnames are most prevalent? Is it the Kim family, the Park family, the Choi family, or the Jo family? You may not know, but there are connected surnames. Isn’t that so? There are many connected surnames. If you rank them as 1, 2, 3, 4, 5… there is a series of ranks centered around you.

Therefore, even though your body was born as the child of someone in this era, the ‘I’ that exists is not just born flatly in this era. Then, the question becomes which qualities of which surnames, which grandmothers and grandfathers, you have inherited the most. If that grandfather’s mother was a Park, then there is a part of that grandfather that resembles the qualities of the Park family. Isn’t that so? This is all mixed in a zigzag manner, and it is all combined to give birth to the person known as ‘me’ today. This is how it is viewed.

If I meet someone and they are a Park, even if it is the first time meeting them, I feel good… Why do I feel good? It is because there were many grandmothers among my ancestors who were of the Park family. When you have many connections to the Park lineage, it naturally feels good. Such connections all exist.
