If you look at your cells, the emotional elements inherited from your ancestors were all different, and adolescence is the time to try to give that connection a movement. Not only to give but also to be able to receive is what makes adolescence good.

Such a time is like spring in the human world. It is a spring garden in the human world. Isn’t that so? Therefore, even if you live your life getting married and having fun, when you think about it in a true sense, you will always long for that youthful boy and girl phase.
At that time, it is a time of freedom. It is a time when one does not take responsibility. If one takes responsibility and is confused, nothing will work out, but at that time, it is a time without responsibility. It is a time when the owner is not determined and one’s position is not decided. At that time, one stands in a position where one can choose freely. Therefore, if one makes a wrong choice during adolescence, it can ruin one’s entire life, and if one makes a good choice, one can live a prosperous life. Such problems arise. Moreover, if descendants make mistakes during their adolescent years, they can completely undermine all the achievements that their ancestors have built up until now.

That is why the sons and daughters of noble families do not marry among themselves. Do you understand? The parents of noble families have been insisting that their children should not choose their partners freely, and there is some validity to that. For example, there are crows and there are egrets, but if an egret were to mate with a crow, would that be acceptable? If they were to have offspring, they would come out all mottled, right? That is why it is necessary to choose carefully.

Conscience is the abode of heaven. To make that choice, what is one method to do so? One must be conscientious. On the right side, there is good, and on the left side, there is evil Satan. That is why we ask, "Are you conscientious?" The position of being conscientious is always horizontal. It is drawing a horizontal line. Conscience has not been distorted. The original nature given by God has not been distorted.

When you do something, you stand at one of three crossroads: whether you are conscientious, unconscientious, or in a good position. This is what is centered and determined. When we say one is conscientious, it means they are standardizing commonality. Therefore, does anyone say that their conscience is distorted? They say it is right, right? That rightness is commonality. And while everyone says that their living environment is commonly right, it is all diverse. It is diverse. When this diversity dances externally, the position of my conscience also tilts into diversity. Conscience is commonly in the right position, but the living environment of humans who possess that conscience is diverse. It can be this way or that way.

Conscience must not follow the movements of the external world. No matter how much the external environment changes, one must adjust it centered on conscience and filter the environment so that it can correspond to conscience in order to walk the good path. However, those who cannot filter the environment and are confused by it will naturally fall into the realm of evil. That is why one must always center on conscience and consider everything as a problem.

The mission of the evangelist and the heart of heaven. What is conscience? It is the abode of heaven. It is the abode of heaven and the abode of hell. Whether it becomes the abode of heaven or the abode of hell depends on the individual and the environment in which they live. Therefore, whenever one acts, it is already determining whether it is good or evil. One must always think about that. When one thinks, is it a thought leaning towards heaven, a thought leaning towards Satan, or a neutral thought that is neither? This is what is determined. It must be that way.

Even when one speaks a word, it is the same. When one calls someone with a simple "Hey," if you think about the root of that word, it depends on whether it was called for one’s own benefit or to benefit that person. If one called that person to use them for their own benefit, then evil is initiated by them. If one called them to benefit that person, then good is brought in.

When one thinks of public matters, God comes in, and when one thinks of private matters, Satan comes in. If you have done something public that others do not know about, do you want to boast about it or not? If you do something extraordinary that everyone will like, you will want to boast about it, right? You want to elevate yourself. Conversely, if you do something shameful, you will want to shrink away. Shrinking away means disappearing, while wanting to boast indicates a promise of thriving.

That is why people are called spiritual beings. If it is good, they will align with good things, and if it is bad, they will align with bad things. If it is bad, they will shrink away. The same goes for danger. If it is dangerous, do you spread your arms and say, "Come on!"? If it is dangerous, you will shrink away without mercy. Even a hedgehog shrinks away when it is in danger. Its body becomes smaller, and its spines stick out. That symbolizes danger.

Liberation means to be completely released. When viewed this way, why is the spring season good? Because spring is a time of release, not a time of binding. The entire universe and all things move in accordance with that relationship. Does a person who is going down a bad path blow a horn? Does a thief blow a horn while going to steal? They all go hiding. If they are going to steal from someone close to them, they will go flat against the ground.

When considering these things, our hearts during adolescence are good. At that time, there is no one who wants to cry. When spring comes, even dandelions bloom, right? Azaleas, cherry blossoms, and all kinds of flowers bloom, and dandelions say, "Do you think you are the only ones with flowers? I have my own flowers too," and they bloom. Just like that, everyone blooms during their adolescent years. Are flowers good or bad? Regardless of the seed, flowers are good. Flowers have a reciprocal relationship with each other and reproduce through giving and receiving. Right? It is exactly the same.

In this way, during adolescence, all the cells of our humanity center around emotional, that is, sentimental areas, and engage in a great cosmic movement to find what is best for themselves. Adolescence is that time. At that time, when one goes to a scenic place, even if the sun sets, one sits there and thinks or becomes lost in contemplation or writes poetry.

People need that kind of state. Everyone likes that kind of state. Even older ladies and gentlemen wish to enter an environment like that of adolescence. You must think about such things. You must realize that heaven is always spring, and God is always spring.

Who is a person who can receive God’s love? A person who can bloom flowers even in winter, summer, and autumn. That is the kind of person one must become. Do you understand what I mean?

That is why the problem lies with you who want to receive heavenly love and establish a connection with heavenly love. It is not about others; it is about you. When you become the problem, what should you do? Bloom the flowers of your heart, and then bloom the flowers of your body. Do you understand? What should you center on? It should not be for the sake of fulfilling your own desires but for the purpose of fulfilling heaven's will... So, stand in the most public position.

How to deal with bad people. What kind of feeling do you always need? You must have the mindset that you are the judge. When something happens, you must discern good from bad. In discerning good and bad, if you want to save the bad, you must hit them, but when you hit them, you should place something good behind it. That way, even if they run away, they will take something good with them. Do you understand? You must strategize like this.

Therefore, even when admonishing or hating someone, do not show a face that simply looks hateful. You must treat them calmly. Isn’t that right? Does a flower frown just because an evil person comes to see it? If it feels bad, of course, it will feel bad. However, flowers simply bloom and emit their fragrance, whether liked or disliked. Similarly, you should not show a bad expression when dealing with bad people. There is a good side even among those bad people.

So, when you speak to such people, how should you do it? You should first refrain from speaking. Encourage them to speak. Ask them how their home is, how their living situation is, whether they have any burdens in their hearts, and whether they are always feeling down. This way, you gently encourage them to talk. Even if you feel uncomfortable with that person, you should still say, "Come on in," and talk about the principles of creation...

Even if you are an investigator examining a sinner, you should use what that sinner can say to say, "Aren’t you like this?" so that they will say, "Yes." Then, ask them to talk about the context surrounding that. When they do not know, ask, "What were your parents like during that time?" and keep asking. Then ask about their siblings, relatives, schoolmates, and how they treated that person. This way, you encourage them to talk a lot. The more they talk, the more it alleviates their burdens.

Even if someone is angry and comes to you with the intention of attacking you, you can subdue them by asking, "What’s wrong with you? Why are you frowning from early morning and showing up here?" If you do that, the situation will fall apart. At that time, ask how they came and talk until everything is resolved. At first, they may be trembling with anger, but the laws of the world do not just go up; they go up and then come down. They come down and then go back up. So, if you push down what has gone up, they will eventually say, "Hehe."

When an unpleasant person comes, try not to speak if possible. If possible, treat them with a peaceful expression. When the other person sees you, you should appear as the person who understands their situation better than anyone else. Do you understand?

When a man is angry and sulking, if a calm young lady appears and smiles beautifully, asking why he is upset, that one word and that expression will dissolve all his anger towards his wife. He thinks, "Ah, I thought all women were like that, but this woman is different." Then he wants to say, "Listen to me," and he shares what he wanted to vent to his wife with her. Because of that conversation, half of his anger is alleviated. It is not a direct venting of anger but an indirect venting that occurs. It should be like that. Even if you have to die, it would be good to say everything you want to say before you die. You must work hard to deal with such people.

You must approach people with a heart to touch them. There are angry people, sulky people, or people who come to deceive you. There are those who lie and deceive themselves. When such a deceiving person comes, you may not know, but the teacher knows. The teacher can already feel it. Such people are obvious. They have a disposition like black ink. A person trying to sneak in with a shady disposition already has a different expression. If they hesitate, you will already know. If they try to speak but hesitate, and if they try to say something but stop, after one, two, or three times, you will think, "Ah, that person has a shady disposition."

You must be able to analyze like that. At that time, you can say, "Oh, how much are you really like that..." and set a trap, saying, "Let’s see how you do." To connect with that person, you must let yourself be deceived. You must let yourself be deceived. You should act as if you know nothing and let yourself be deceived. Once you let yourself be deceived, that person will find it enjoyable. In this busy world, who remembers who knows that person? So, when I go as an evangelist from the perspective of someone who does not know, it becomes the second time. The second time, they come with that same disposition. Then you let yourself be deceived again. After being deceived a few times, while I may be wary of that person, they will like me and come to find me. You must be willing to let yourself be deceived a few times. However, that does not mean you should give them the door to your house. (Laughter) You cannot give them that, but you can play a game where you give them something to use.

If you do that, that person will fulfill their wish and go back. After doing that once, twice, or three times, when they come back, you can ask, "What did you spend the money you took last time on?" Then you can say, "When you came here, you must have come with bad thoughts, wanting to use people and fulfill your own desires. I have already yielded to you once, twice, and three times, but are you still going to do that?" They will bow their heads at that point.

That is when you can confront them. You do not hit them, of course. (Laughter) You must approach them with the heart of a parent who loves their child, handling them through emotional connections. You should treat them with a motherly heart. If you say, "From your perspective, am I not like a younger sister to you? Of course, you must have come to me with that younger sisterly heart," that one word will turn them around. 

That is why you must speak with emotional content. Both people and animals like emotional areas. Even dogs like it when you show them affection. Right? When you try to give a foal medicine, you cannot force it. I once saw someone giving medicine to a foal, and the owner held the foal’s neck gently, fed it something delicious, and stroked it to open its mouth before giving it the medicine. (Laughter) It is the same. If you tell it to come while hitting it, it will never come. Right? You must call it while stroking it. Right? That is the principle of the world. That is how governance works. Therefore, when advising a misguided person, you must do it in that way. However, some church leaders say, "I am the church leader; how can I not recognize the elder and do such things?" This is a failing grade, a failing grade. (Laughter) In terms of scores, it is like minus fifty points. 

When a person is lonely, it is sad. At that time, everyone generally wants sympathy. Seeking support is a human tendency. That is how the human world works. At that time, you must become the closest person to them. If he is a man and you are also a man, you should be friendly like an older brother from the position of a younger brother.
Treating them kindly, "Honestly, am I not in such and such a position right now? When I look at my circumstances and your circumstances, isn't your situation better than mine? If you are my elder brother, you have the responsibility to support, nurture, and guide someone like me who is in a younger sibling's position. How can you, as an elder brother, act in a way that is less than that of a younger sibling?" This is what I am saying. When one is in the position of an elder brother, they should advise with that mindset. You must use materials that are close to the emotional realm to guide that person. Even if a parent strikes a child with a whip, the child quickly forgets being hit by the parent. Isn't that right? I've seen it myself; after receiving a scolding, when the parents later say, "Oh, are you okay?" the child has already forgotten everything. But when siblings scold each other, do they forget or not? They hold onto it. That's how it works. Therefore, what is the great saying in the principles of the Unification Church? It is, "With the heart of a parent, using the body of a servant, let us shed tears for humanity, sweat for the earth, and shed blood for heaven." There is no one who does not resonate with this saying, and there is no being that does not resonate with it. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That saying is indeed a great one. From my experience, that is how it is.

**Evangelism and Love**
When the teacher has walked this path to this extent, what kind of people has he not met? He has encountered swindlers, robbers, all sorts of people. Although such people have now fallen away, there is no one who dislikes the founder of the Unification Church. Do you understand what I mean? They may oppose the Unification Church in their own way, but do they oppose it because they dislike the teacher? They oppose it because they dislike someone like Yoo Hyun-won. (Laughter) They oppose it not because they hate the teacher. Because of the emotional connections that have been sown, they cannot move on without resolving them. 

Therefore, before one can reap those connections, they must have a deeper heart. The emotional standard that the teacher has sown cannot be removed by anyone. Thus, those who leave the Unification Church, even if they marry and live well, as time goes on, they will gradually develop a sense of longing. They will think, "I thought this path was fun, but it isn't. I need to go back." This happens. Even if they dislike the Unification Church, the teacher appears in their dreams and says, "Hey, you shouldn't do that." This kind of thing continues to happen. Why? Because it has been planted with heart. Therefore, without having a deeper heart, one cannot reap it.

A child who has received parental love must feel a love that surpasses the love they received from their parents to break free from that standard. If they cannot feel it, there is no way to uproot that standard. Isn't that right? This is how it works. 

When we look at the restoration providence, today's world of Satan is filled with emotional problems that have become chronic. Whether it is between father and mother, husband and wife, or children, even to distant relatives, these issues are tightly woven into chronic pain, and this must be uprooted. Do you understand? As I mentioned earlier, to shed the love connection established between parents and children, one must possess a stronger force of love; otherwise, they cannot break free. Similarly, to completely shed the emotional content connected to the world of Satan and to emerge from it, one must manifest a stronger force of love. That is the principle.

That is why Jesus said, "Love me more than anyone else." This does not mean that Jesus is starving for love and wants to be loved. It means, "I love you more than anyone else, so you should love me more." Do you understand? The love that people in the world of Satan give is of a high caliber. We must create the motivation and foundation that allows us to give such love. Then, even if we are told not to love, we will love.

Therefore, what is evangelism? Evangelism is to abandon the world of Satan and guide people to follow the heavenly path with a smile. It is to lead them to the Kingdom of Heaven. This is what you must understand. Do you understand? When you look at evangelism, you see people trying to bring others in regardless of whether they like them or not, saying "Come, come." That will not work. People are spiritual beings, so you must pray for a specific person and experiment with that. Love one specific person deeply and shed tears with a heart of pain to bring them before the purpose. You must study this.

When you go out to evangelize, wandering around on your own saying, "Oh, the Principle, the creation principle, the theory of happiness is like this. It’s good to believe in the Unification Church. It’s good," you may speak well, but that alone is not enough. If there is someone who is a strong person, you must pray for that strong person. The issue is how to go beyond the love that their parents have for them. This is a struggle. How can I possess a heart that surpasses that of their mother and father to win them over? That is the issue.

Because people are spiritual beings, they do not want to go to places that lead to destruction but want to follow places that lead to prosperity. Therefore, the question is how to make that person feel a love that is more beneficial than what their parents feel for them. This is not worldly love.

**The Heart is the Foundation of the Universe**
Which comes first, existence or life? Answer me. Today, even in philosophy, the question of ontology is being discussed: which comes first, existence or life? Did life arise because there is existence, or does existence come from life? This will become an important question in future philosophy. Answer me. Did existence come first, or did life come first? 

Today's philosophy starts from existence. It does not touch upon life. Where does life come from? Life does not arise on its own; it comes from the love of parents. The world of life and the world of love are the realms managed by God. Do you understand? What is below that is what humans are currently touching upon in their philosophical thoughts.

That is why life precedes existence. What moves existence is the power of life. What moves life? Only love can move life. This is because life started from love, and it moves according to the connections of love and seeks the results of love. Theoretically, that is how it works. You must keep this in mind. Thus, emotional issues become the foundation of the creation of the universe. In light of this, love is at the center. Do you understand?

**God's Love is Like Yeast**
If you observe a person who is bound, you will find that they are receiving the love of their mother and father. When a person is receiving the love of their parents and the love of their siblings, it becomes difficult for them to evangelize. You must be able to sense that. For such a person, you must present something that can be beneficial. You must present something that can be advantageous to them. However, just presenting it is not enough. You must evoke the feelings of love and create a relationship with them.

To do this, you need a love that is like yeast. The Bible speaks of yeast metaphorically, right? That love that is like yeast is God's love. How do I feel God's love? I have said to pray for one life, but you should pray for a specific person. Pray for that person through the night. Those who have experienced the pain of losing a son or daughter know how heart-wrenching it is. Isn't that right? "Yes." Those who have raised children and lost them understand that heart. If one loves beyond that heart, anyone will be drawn in.

And what you must understand is that when a person dies, do they go to heaven or hell? They go to hell. They are afflicted with the disease that leads them to hell. Their legs rot, their arms rot, and they die in such a state. How devastating it must be for parents to see such people! That feeling is precisely God's feeling.

Therefore, you must have the potential to possess a heart that surpasses that. Those with good ancestors naturally feel such a heart. Are there people who are very emotional? The descendants of those who cry a lot do not perish. Just wait and see. Look for it. The descendants of those who cry a lot do not perish. However, the descendants of those who do not cry do perish.

**If You Love More than Their Parents, Anyone Can Be Guided**
Therefore, if you love someone more strongly than their mother and father do, that person will be drawn to you even if they say not to come. Do you understand? It is a battle of love. Evangelism must be done in this way. You must become a being through whom they can feel more love than they do from their parents. This is the source of life.

To do this, how can you make that person feel love that surpasses that of their mother and father? That is why you pray. It is utterly impossible for a human being alone, so to save one life, you must invest your heart. From a principled perspective, God is the subject, and I am the object. Therefore, I must enter the position of the object before the subject, the perfect love of God, in a completely humble position. I must enter the position of a sacrificial offering. Do you understand?

While striking my own body and losing myself... Sacrificing myself to the point of being willing to die for my child is the heart of a parent, so I must feel a sense of fulfillment in sacrificing myself for that person. Then, what must I do as the object before the subject, God? I cannot just pray to God as I am. I must stand in the position of humility. "I am lacking. I have nothing." Then I enter the realm of the horizontal line. Do you understand? To reach such a position, you must invest all your heart and pray.

When you are willing to sacrifice your life and invest your heart for one person, God will work. Your entire heart must resonate with the heart that admires God's love. In other words, the heart you had during your adolescence, longing for all connections, must blossom for God to begin to move. Do you understand what I mean?

You must enter such a realm in your prayers. When you enter that realm, there will be no one you cannot feel a connection with. From this perspective, if you feel pity for all people, they will line up, and among them, the wicked will be seen at the forefront, shackled and dragged to hell. You will also see each one tumbling from the edge of a cliff into the abyss. God works in this way. To elevate emotional stimulation and the authority of the heart, He shows visions and provides stimulating connections. Thus, when you hold onto that person with a heart that surpasses that of their parents, regardless of the dangers and difficulties that lie ahead, even if your hands and body are torn apart, when you strongly declare that you will save them, God will work. God does not work in trivial matters but only in strong, ultimate circumstances.

That is why, without such experiences and connections, no matter how much you evangelize, you cannot create a family that can determine life and death. This is the principle of heaven, and the teacher knows this.

When the teacher himself was establishing his purpose, what kind of heart did he have? He had that principle. When you pray for one person and invest your heart, even if someone has lived a fun life through romantic relationships and marriages, if they experience a love that is more profound and three-dimensional than God's love or their own love, whether it is a husband or wife, they will turn around. They will completely turn around, and when their previously connected spouse appears before them, they will feel as if a snake has appeared. When their spouse comes and tries to hold their hand, they will feel as if a poisonous snake is about to bite them. At that moment, they realize how conflicting God's love is with human love. Do you understand what I mean?

When people in the world see with ordinary eyes, they may boast that their spouse is beautiful, but when they enter that realm, they do not see beauty. They see a poisonous snake. They feel as if the snake, with its venom, is opening its mouth and rushing towards them. That feeling arises. Do you understand? That is why it is a battle of love. You must understand this.

**What Moves Life is Love**
No matter how strong a person may be, if I am stronger, they will be drawn to me, just like a lodestone. When centered on God's love, if you love... On a cold winter day, if a stove is radiating warmth, will people gather around the warm stove or not? Even if you tell them not to gather, they will. Just like all insects are drawn to light, we must move life centered on the powerful love of God. What moves life? Love. The foundation of that love is God's love. When we manifest God's love, there is no life that does not move. You must experiment with this.

When the teacher came down to Busan Yeongdo, he stood at the pinnacle of his life. It was the most serious moment in his life, so he could love his comrades, brothers, and people more than anyone else. At that time, the teacher's entire being was focused, and God was also in a state of love, seeking one child, forming a family, and finding a nation, so he spoke with the feelings that God felt.

At that time, those words were not my words. They were words spoken through a microphone. At that time, everyone who came would enter the spiritual realm within a week. What is a week? Within a few hours, there were experiences of the spiritual world. It was like sending a broadcast to the earth. It was like sending a broadcast of God's love. Because that broadcast spread out into the world, those who longed for such gifts in the spiritual realm were electrified and came back again. Such events occurred.

Therefore, you must establish such standards. Even if you do not go directly, do not see, and do not meet, you can already feel the spiritual standards and connections. For those who have inherited high spiritual standards from their ancestors, it happens automatically, just like when the sun rises in the morning, whether far away or close, everyone welcomes the sun. Thus, you will find such connections and meet them in your prayers. 

Have you ever been so crazy about longing for God?
So, how much have you longed for God, how much have you longed to meet Jesus, to the point where your eyes well up with tears? That's the issue. Speaking as a teacher, there were times when I missed God so much that I stayed awake for more than a week, praying through the night. I would squint my eyes in the morning just to see the sunlight... There were times like that. You have to be filled with such longing. Otherwise, you will enter a serious situation where you cannot completely resolve the issue of life and death, whether I live as a human or die. However, you cannot just die. You cannot die without value. Therefore, you must enter a serious problem of fundamentally resolving the issue of life and death and negotiate with God.

God is the highest being, the subject of all things. Speaking of love, He is the subject of love; speaking of ideals, He is the subject of ideals; and since He is the subject of the origin of all existence, isn't it our human duty to love that subject more than anyone else? Even if vaguely, you should have the thought that you want to see Him, that you want to hear His words, that you want to eat and live together with Him, and you should be filled with that longing to the point of madness.

But if your eyes go one way and your hands go another, can you just say, "Oh, I love God"? It has to be one. Then your heart will straighten. That’s why those who have met the teacher and received grace cannot forget the teacher even after death. They follow him wherever he goes. Those who do not are not part of the Unification Church. When the teacher goes on a world tour, those who just think, "He'll be back," are not connected to the teacher. Such people will become even more distant in the spirit world.

280 The Mission of the Evangelist and the Heart of Heaven
Whether beautiful or ugly, it is my form
Is there an old man here? If you go to the headquarters, there is an old lady. She is so wrinkled that you can't even imagine how ugly she is. In the world, there probably isn't an old lady who is as ugly as she is, no matter how old she gets. But from the first time I met her, she knew where the teacher would go at night and came early in the morning to sit in the best spot to guard it. When the teacher suddenly appears, she greets him first, saying, "Oh, teacher, are you coming down?" She is so ugly that even if she greets him, it feels unlucky. (Laughter) Ah, whether in the morning or evening, whenever I enter the room, that old lady is the first to greet.

That doesn’t mean I dislike her. Ideally, it should be the younger people who do that, but she is always at the forefront. So one day, I scolded that old lady, saying, "If this old woman is going to die, she should die properly. What is this? Every morning, the teacher appears looking young, and this is just ridiculous. Just don’t show up and go away." I scolded her like that. How hurtful it must have been for her. Even though she is risking her life like that, the teacher does not recognize her... "Oh, what am I living for!" she must have thought... If I had said that to the young ladies, it would have been a big deal. But since she is nearly seventy years old, it was okay.

So I prayed to God, saying, "Whether I die or live, please take my life." I prayed, "How frustrating it must be for the teacher to see my ugly face! Oh, Father, take me away. If not, please move the teacher's heart and touch him." (Laughter) I fasted and prayed for more than three days, crying and sobbing. I prayed while crying, and later I heard a response from God, and that response was truly remarkable. He said, "Hey, the person called Moon is the main character of the Principle, and isn't there a duality in the Principle? Therefore, you know that men and women resemble God? 

281 
So whether beautiful or ugly, it is my form." (Laughter) That was a brilliant answer. "Whether beautiful or ugly, it is my form. Therefore, the teacher, who loves all forms of God, will never hate you. From today, it's okay for you to do as you used to." (Laughter) After a few days, that old lady didn’t show up, but one morning when I came out, she was sitting there grinning. I shouted, "Oh, what is this old lady doing from the morning?" and she said, "Even if the teacher scolds me, I am happy." (Laughter) Then she said, "Oh, the teacher said this and that about me, so I prayed to God, asking Him to either kill me or save me, and I received the answer that whether ugly or beautiful, it is my form, so the teacher can never hate me. Is that true?" (Laughter) Now, I got caught by that old lady. Would I say that’s not true, or would I agree? So I said, "Hey, that’s a brilliant answer." (Laughter)

From then on, wherever the teacher was going, she would know in advance and would go ahead and wait. But that doesn’t make her unlikable. It would be difficult if everyone did that. Also, when there is a special gathering or event, if there are too many people, the venue becomes cramped, and only certain people like district leaders or church leaders are asked to gather. When they say only those people should come, uninvited guests are not welcomed. So when they are told not to come, they feel hurt. Seeing that, such people always want to be near the teacher.

In terms of age, the teacher is the same age as her son. And why does she like the teacher so much, even though he is not handsome? The teacher has small eyes and is not good-looking. What kind of love is God's love?
God's love is parental love and children's love. Parental love begins first, and then children's love begins. Do you understand? Therefore, what you should first feel when you enter the Unification Church is parental love. When you feel parental love, the antenna of your heart rises. Then you will know all of God's work. The prophets belong to that realm.

How did the fall happen? It happened because we could not establish a relationship with God centered on the Father. We humans must become the sons and daughters of God. Do you understand? Therefore, to become the sons and daughters of God, what must happen first?
The love of parents must be manifested on this earth. After the love of parents centered on God is shown, the love of children is realized. Children are born from their parents and are nurtured as children to form a family of love between husband and wife. 

Children must receive the love of their parents, and parents must love their children. This is vertical love. You need to understand this. The love exchanged between parents and children is the love of a parent-child relationship. This is vertical love. Do you understand? However, vertical love alone cannot establish the relative forms of inside and outside; this is the principle of heaven and earth. Since there is no existence that transcends the foundation of subject and object, if there is no vertical subject and horizontal object, it cannot endure.

What is the vertical love we speak of? It is the love of the parent-child relationship. It refers to the love that parents have for their children and the love that children exchange with their parents. This is called vertical love. Therefore, even if one cannot share secrets with their spouse, one can share secrets with their son. In other words, a wife is considered a stranger. This is vertical love.

So, what do we call someone without a mother or father? "An orphan." Is it said that orphans are lovely or ugly? It means they are lonely. Why are orphans lonely? Because they have no one to lean on and no one to rely on. It means there is no center. Here, when we say vertical, we refer to speaking about a center. Without a center, one's value of existence cannot be established. Therefore, to be lonely means to be in a dangerous position.

When vertical love is completely exchanged and you and I become one, only then can we say that the sons and daughters have matured. Do you understand? When sons and daughters can completely exchange love with their parents as mature individuals, only then are they ready to be married off. So, what does getting married mean? It means engaging in horizontal love. Vertical love is the parent-child relationship, while horizontal love is the husband-wife relationship. That is how it works.

When a child is born between a couple, what is stronger: the parents' willingness to sacrifice for their child or the willingness of the couple to sacrifice for each other? It is stronger for the couple to sacrifice for each other, right? "No." Then, is it true that the parents' willingness to sacrifice for their child is stronger? Really? "Yes." Really? "Yes." Vertical love is stronger. From this perspective, the love between couples is weaker than the love between parents and children.

However, where does the power for a child born between a couple come from? It starts weak but becomes strong in the outcome. You need to understand that. The love of parents is vertical love. Love always follows the path of the natural forces of the universe. The love for children is inherently strong because it exists within the realm of subjective vertical love.

In other words, where does the power that allows parents to love their sons and daughters more come from? It comes from God. Jesus also said, “When I was hungry, you gave me something to eat, and when I was in prison, you visited me.” The disciples asked, “When did we give you something to eat when you were hungry, and when did we visit you in prison?” At that time, Jesus said, “What you did for the least of these brothers of mine, you did for me.” You need to understand that.

When you walk down the street and see a beggar lying there because of discomfort, you must discover the feeling that your mother or father is lying sick because of you. That grandfather who is tired and has collapsed could be my father. If he were my father, what would I do? I must find a way to serve him as my closest person. Do you understand what I mean?

Study human emotions so that you can become close to anyone. When I was in Japan long ago, there was an incident. In Akasaka, Japan, it rains often. One day, I got on a tram wearing wet clothes. I often went to the labor site. I would throw off my student uniform, put on work clothes, and put black paint on my face, then intentionally move to sit next to a girl. (Laughter) When I asked the girl next to me, “Where are you going?” she looked at me in disbelief. I tested whether the heart of a girl in nice clothes was genuine or fake. (Laughter) When the tram shook, I would stand close and step on her foot without caring, and she would scream, “Ouch!” and get angry. I often did that. That’s a way of restoration. Sometimes there are truly good girls. Instead, the girl would feel sorry. Then I would feel sorry in return. If there was a handsome man, I would often play that game with him. I analyzed and criticized human psychology a lot.

Sometimes, if I had something to give, I wouldn’t go and politely hand it over. I would throw it in a way that would make the person feel bad. I would give it with a face like an enemy. That’s all research. Until now, I have lived that kind of life.

That’s why wherever I go, I’m not someone who just blends in. Even if I go to the labor site, within 30 minutes, I make all the people working there my friends. No matter how rough they look, I know their personalities. I think, “This person has such a personality, so they must be difficult…” Then I poke them in the stomach and say, “You have this kind of greed.” They would respond, “How did you know that?” I would say, “How would I know? Do you know if your wife and I are related?” That’s how I would proceed. Then they would ask, “How do you know?” I would say, “How do I know, you rascal?” In fact, I don’t know who their wife is or who their in-laws are. This arouses curiosity, and even if they stay quiet, they would come to me. If I did that in the morning and then sat quietly alone during lunchtime without bringing lunch… I would have already formed a connection. They would come and say, “Why are you sitting alone?” I would say, “I don’t feel like eating.” They would invite me to eat together. “Even if we eat together, it will only be barley rice and soybean paste. Ugh, that’s unpleasant.” But already, we would be getting close. Within 30 minutes, we would become friends. First, you need to get close to people to be able to work.

When I go to the porters, I quickly become friends with them. I also get along well with grandmothers. They say it’s really fun to talk with me. The grandmothers also fall head over heels for me. Why is that? Because I have a lot of experience. I have a lot of experience observing and examining human relationships.

If I were to use what I have observed and experienced to exploit someone, I would get punched. The reason I played those games with those people was that I thought I needed to pave the way for good deeds in the future. I did that from a public standpoint.

Collect life materials through all experiences. In the past, I walked around the streets of Seoul dressed as a woman for three days. (Laughter) The hardest part was holding onto the hem of my skirt. Can a man walk around like that? So, I had no choice but to choose a rainy day and spent three days like that. I tied a towel around my head, dressed up as a woman, and walked around the streets. Everything in life is fascinating. Wherever I go, if there’s an old man who is shoveling dung, I don’t just pass by. While everyone else is blocking their noses because of the smell, I wonder how that grandfather’s nose is shaped that he can’t smell it. What’s going on with that grandfather’s nose? I’m curious about that. It’s strange. So I ask, “Grandfather, can you smell it or not?” He replies, “It does smell.” Then I ask, “Is the smell good or bad?” He says, “It’s neither good nor bad.” Can he say it’s bad? That’s just how it is.

Sometimes when I go to the countryside, I see people working with manure. In Gangwon-do, using manure in corn fields makes the corn grow best. Anyone who has farmed in the countryside knows this. Try it once. Manure is the best. The big ears of corn grow like a big broom. To dry this manure, you have to lay it out and spread it to dry. In my hometown, my brother used to sit like that. I thought the worst thing in the world was dung, but he was trying to pick up the biggest pieces first, stirring around. Think about it. When you handle dung, it slips through your fingers… (Laughter) How can one do that? Could I do that? If you try it, you can do it. It’s also fun. If you think of it as work, the smell doesn’t matter. When you get absorbed in work, you forget about the smell. That’s how it works.

That’s why life, living in this world, has many interesting and wonderful things. From there, you study everything and gather materials to prepare for the future, to build a big house. I have a lot of such experiences.

So when I go to the countryside, I know how to farm, and when I go to the seaside, I know how to fish. Even when I throw a net, I have to go out when the rooster crows at dawn. If I’m going to do it, I do it with the conviction that I will record it. I go out when the first rooster crows and do that work until it’s bright dawn. I always have the principle that I will not be a loser in the world. I have the mindset that I will never lose, no matter where I go or what I do. That’s why I never lose to others. I feel the same way when I put in effort.

You must know how to make the flower of the heart bloom. The teacher has experienced all these life processes centered on God. You need to tell stories from your experiences to make it feel real. Do you understand? You need to talk about what you have experienced for the audience to feel it. If you lie, it won’t feel real.

God is the same. That’s why you must adapt everything and lead God. If you want to love God, the question is how can I feel God’s love? Because love is what moves life, and it is the principle of love to move life, the question is how much of God’s love I can embody.

You need to understand the reason why you are not able to evangelize. It’s not because of others; the problem lies within yourself. If there are roses blooming beautifully on the street, there’s no passerby who wouldn’t be interested in those flowers. Is that right? There’s no one who wouldn’t be interested, right? “There’s no one.” It’s the same for everyone. You should be like a blooming rose in front of people, radiating fragrance. If an animal passes by, it might get hurt. I should pick it and put it in the living room.” Similarly, you must become someone who knows how to bloom such emotional flowers. Do you understand? It’s like how insects are attracted to a light at night.

Three days ago, a lady brought a pot of chrysanthemums to commemorate the arrival of Japanese family members. At that time, all the flowers were standing straight, but when I returned from the countryside, sadly, all the flowers were (gesturing) like this, like this. One was like this, and another was like this… They tilted to catch the morning sunlight but couldn’t return and just stayed like that. In the evening sunlight, they were bowed down and bent. Think about it. Isn’t it true that all life tends to turn toward the sunlight? Isn’t that right? Even the humble plants do that, and because God’s love is the sun of all life in the universe, when it manifests with that love, there’s nothing that doesn’t want to connect.

When I was in prison, I kept my mouth shut and didn’t say a word. There were many communists in the world, and if I said one wrong word, my neck would be on the line. I didn’t speak, but the spirits of my ancestors in the spiritual world liked me. Do you understand? Because the spirits in the spiritual world liked me, they informed my descendants, “Hey, you must take care of Master Moon here.” That’s how I ended up with dozens of disciples without saying a word. If I had spoken, how many disciples would I have had? When I start speaking, I don’t know whether it’s day or night. I don’t think about whether it’s night.

The mindset an evangelist must have. When you think about all this, where is the problem? Don’t blame anyone. The reason you can’t evangelize is not because of Master Moon of the Unification Church. Master Moon of the Unification Church is a global champion when viewed from the perspective of the purpose. There’s no doubt about it.

If you have received education under such a master, you must do as he says. If you do that, it will definitely work out. But first, you yourself are not enough. You cannot go around trying to evangelize others while leaving your own self behind. First, I must be clean. I must first be complete before the purpose. I must be complete. In terms of electricity, I must become a conductor with no resistance so that electricity can flow well. If that happens, there will be no resistance. Electricity does not flow to places with a lot of resistance; it flows to places with no resistance. Isn’t that right?

That’s why you must be pure. Observe the pure people and the harsh people in your life. If you watch them for a month, two months, or a year, the results will definitely show. If you are sincere, no matter what anyone says, good results will definitely appear. Therefore, you must understand that the reason you are not able to evangelize is not because of those people but because of yourself. Do you understand? The problem lies within you.

When you deal with people, there are good people and people you dislike, right? That’s right? There are good people and people you dislike. Why do you dislike some people? It’s because that person tries to deal with me centered on themselves, asserting their own interests and trying to make it a one-way street. Such people will definitely become unpleasant. This is true even in the world. Even among couples, if the husband only thinks of himself, it becomes unpleasant. This is worse than a honey pig or a bear. When that happens, there will definitely be backlash.

That’s why people who do not prioritize themselves and seek public interest will inevitably be liked by everyone. They are liked because they benefit others. This is the principle. Therefore, you must always have a sense of public interest.

How should you have a sense of public interest? You must have the heart of a parent.
give it to someone else. If you received 5,000 won from your husband, you should set aside your own food expenses and put the rest back in the envelope to give to someone else. This is the mindset you should have. 

You must think about what kind of attitude you should have as a missionary. If you are living in a community and someone is struggling, you should be the first to help them without expecting anything in return. This is the essence of living for others. 

When you give, don't think about how much you have given or expect to receive something back. The true spirit of giving comes from a heart that feels sorry for not being able to give more. This is the heart of a parent, always wanting to do more for their children. 

You should strive to live in such a way that you forget what you have given and remember only what you have received. This is the principle of living for others. If you have a heart that is always ready to give, you will never be in want. 

Remember, those who are always wanting more for themselves will ultimately find themselves in a place of lack. But those who live to give will always find abundance in their lives. 

As you reflect on these teachings, consider how you can embody this spirit in your daily life. How can you be a source of support and love for those around you? This is the challenge and the calling of every missionary.

The teacher has a lot of money right now. There is indeed money. However, I am stingy for myself. The teacher has trained himself this way. I never spend for myself. I do not buy what I need. However, when it comes to public work, I do not hesitate to spend. I consider it something that must be used.

Right now, the headquarters probably has not a single penny. Still, I do not worry. I need to spend several tens of millions of won each month. This month, I need to have 150 million won. Even though I do not have a single penny right now, I do not worry. This will all be resolved. Isn't that strange? However, because God is not dead... Isn't that right? You must create a foundation before doing anything. You check whether there is certainty or not. At such times, God asks, "Do you have the capacity to match the rhythm there?" It is the teacher’s wish that church leaders become the model case for such men. Do you feel bad about it, or do you like it? "I like it." If you like it, then you should do it.

And among the members living together, there are people you don’t want to see, right? There is at least one such person. Who is that person? That person is the central figure who decides whether you can bring grace or not. You must handle that person well. Do you understand? If you touch that person wrongly, it will cause anger, but if you handle that person well, it will bring blessings. 

Therefore, if there is a troublesome woman, you should handle her carefully. 

Everyone, do you know that at the military academy, if a cadet is boycotted by a woman while dating, they are immediately expelled? How can a man who cannot handle one woman become a commander responsible for the lifeline of the Republic of Korea? If the military academy of Korea is like that, what can a church leader of the Unification Church, who is in a position responsible for managing the world, do if he cannot handle about ten women? Such people should be executed. What do you think? Is the teacher’s statement correct or not? "It is correct." Women may feel bad, but it cannot be helped. Handling women is simple. If you go to the market and there is no cream when you come back, buy some and bring it. Wrap it nicely and give it to them. It doesn’t cost much. When you come back from somewhere, call them and say you bought this for them to use, and it’s not expensive, so use it without burden. If you do that a few times, the hearts of women will turn well. You need to study such things.

You also need to study the personalities of women. Women usually have hysteria several times a month. They sometimes pretend to be depressed and act strangely. At such times, if that woman is sleeping in the cold room, you should cover her with the blanket she was using. If she seems to be feeling unwell, you should cover her gently. Then, in the morning, pray for our lady to be blessed. Try doing this; will it get worse?

To become a master, you must know how to serve ten people. Otherwise, it won’t work. You cannot lead absolutely. Therefore, when you return to your respective churches this time, you must unite with the church members and become two wheels, one right and one left, so that you can roll well. If you roll like that and gain speed, it won’t matter if you bump into a big house, and if you bump into a big rock, you will break that rock. Therefore, if you go out united, you will surely develop. This is the teacher’s view.

Now, the day you have to return home is not far away. What will you do? It’s a big deal, isn’t it? Is it a big deal or not? "It is a big deal." So, do not do everything alone but work together with the church leader. You must always join forces with the church leader and with each other to lay the foundation before returning.

In the future, when you return to your regions, you must be concerned about the urgent situation of this era and the fact that Kim Il-sung is targeting South Korea, and you must move collectively. Men should stand on one side and women on the other, connected like a mesh, so that they can withstand anything that comes their way with generosity and courage, expanding the foundation of the church, which will also elevate the dignity of women and the dignity of the men responsible for the church. Only then can we establish a condition to fulfill the will before heaven, and that is why the teacher hopes that you will do so. Do you understand? "Yes."

Church leaders, please do not become men that women dislike, and evangelists, do not become women that men dislike. If you stand in a position where you can like each other and God’s love descends upon you, then heaven will surely work there, and all sorts of strange things will happen. This is the fact that the teacher knows. If such things do not happen even while doing this, then the teacher is a fake. So, try it and see if it’s true or not. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

With such a heart, if men and women pray together, even the sick will be healed. Heaven works. Knowing this, and returning with such conditions, if you can part with the people of that neighborhood with tears without damaging the dignity of the Unification Church, there will be many ways for heaven to leave that foundation after your return. I sincerely hope that you will leave a model of working harmoniously together. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Beloved Father, your children who have been working in the four provinces connected to Seoul have gathered here and are now about to return.

Father, even if there may not be a time to meet again with those we met this time, please protect them. Father, love the lonely daughters who are out on the front lines. Every time I see the pitiful appearance of the young children who are separated from their mothers, I feel sad, but I realize that they must walk this path. When I think of the husbands who must take their children to work from a place of extraordinary concern, I know well how miserable that situation is.

If you have a heart of compassion for this place, if you have a heart that wants to sympathize with this place, please remember that we are walking this path because we want you to love this nation before loving the Unification family.

Father, there is a path that must be walked. There is a responsibility that must be fulfilled even if it means death. Father, even if we are old, we must walk, and even if we are young, there is a fateful path that must be walked. Father, we know that we have a historical mission that must be fulfilled with all our strength and at any cost for the day of the liberation of our homeland. It is okay if one of us falls, but when I think that the nation and the people must not perish, we must not become unfilial children before your tremendous wish. Therefore, please let us be true sons and daughters who are not ashamed to receive your love and who can be praised forever in history by being filial before you and loyal to the nation, equipped with the loyalty of heaven.

Father, I know better than anyone that they are in difficult circumstances. However, since there is no nation where you can rest yet, we know the circumstances of the Father who had no choice but to bear the historical responsibility for a long time and spend tedious days.

We know that offerings are made not from what is left over after eating but from the place of sacrificing life. Therefore, we are a pitiful group that continues this path while maintaining our lives, so please remember us, Father. I believe that you will have compassion for the pitiful cries of this group. Just as you protected me when I was in such a situation, I am sure that you will protect and guard the path these people are taking.

Please let them be your sons and daughters who can advance against evil, equipped with the glory of sons, standing confidently with the authority of heaven and affirming the values of victory in the dark valley of death.

Today, I have spoken about the responsibilities of the evangelist and the mission of heaven, and what it means to carry the heart of heaven. I earnestly ask that you bless us to prepare an environment that can please you until we meet again, using this connection. 

Father, now let the footsteps of those who are going forth be steps to leave behind your will and your desire. May their tearful hearts guide their path, and may the tearful stories that can testify to your heart be connected to the families and townspeople they encounter.

Father, please reveal your glory this month and this year. Block all the paths that the masterminds of the North wish to take, and at this urgent moment when we must expand the foundation of your glory, let us be your sons and daughters who do not feel ashamed before your will, putting all our intelligence and efforts into preparing that place without holding back.

May your grace be with those who are going, and may your infinite blessings be upon the families and children connected to them. I earnestly ask that the day of victory that the Unification family desires for this nation and this people may come soon, and I pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> I think it will take a few months when I go this time. While the teacher is away, I ask you to fight well with dedication and feel a sense of accomplishment without any accidents. Do you understand? "Yes."
